 						{{# if(d.resList){ layui.each(d.resList, function(index, item0){ }}
                      	<div class="layui-row layadmin-homepage-text-center">

<script>
var tableObjPlDHDorms;
var tableObjPlDHDormSele;
layui.use(['easytable','form','laydate','easyutils','tableMerge','step'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,table=layui.table
  ,easytable = layui.easytable
  ,form = layui.form
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils
  ,laydate = layui.laydate
  ,tableMerge = layui.tableMerge
  ,step = layui.step;
  
  laydate.render({
    elem: '#DormBedplDh_BEGIN_DATE'
    ,format: 'yyyy-MM-dd'
    ,value: easyutils.getNowFormatDate()
    ,done: function(value, date, endDate){
       
    }
  });
  
    step.render({
      elem: '#dormPlDhStepId',
      filter: 'dormPlDhStepFilter',
      width: '100%', //设置容器宽度
      stepWidth: '750px',
      height: '1000px',
      stepItems: [{
          title: '查找须对换学生'
      },{
          title: '查找被对换学生'
      },{
          title: '确认对换'
      },{
          title: '完成'
      }]
    });
  
  	  form.on('submit(first_dHformStep)', function (data) {
		var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
		var checkStatus = table.checkStatus('tablePLDHSUTID'),checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
		if(checkStatus.isAll && checkData.length!=1){
			easyutils.layMes('error',"不能全选！");
			return false;
		}
        if(checkData.length === 0){
      		easyutils.layMes('error',"请选择数据！");
      		return false;
      	}
	    var oldBedUids="",stuUids="",stuNames="",sexCode="",isSame=0;  
	    var num = 0;
	    layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){ 
	    	oldBedUids+=item.BED_UID+",";
	    	stuUids+=item.STU_INFO_UID+",";
	    	stuNames+=item.STUDENT_NAME+",";
	    	if(sexCode!=null&&sexCode!=''){
	    		if(sexCode != item.ROOM_SEX){
	    			isSame=1;
	    		}
	    	}
	    	sexCode=item.ROOM_SEX;
	    	num+=1;
	  	}); 
	    if(isSame==1){
	    	easyutils.layMes('error',"所选要对换床位的学生的性别不一致，请选择同一性别的学生！");
      		return false;
		}
	
	    layui.$("#PLDH_OLD_BED_UIDS").val(oldBedUids);
	    //layui.$("#PLDH_STU_INFO_UIDS").val(stuUids);
	    layui.$("#PLDH_SEL_STUDENTS_NAME").val(stuNames);
	    layui.$("#PLDH_OLD_BED_NUMS").val(num);
	    
	    layui.$("#Q_PLDHSelect_ROOM_SEX").val(sexCode);
	    layui.$("#Q_PLDHSelect_BED_UIDS").val(oldBedUids);
	    $("#btn_PLDHSelect_search").click();
	    
	  	step.next('#dormPlDhStepId');
    	return false;
	  });
	
	  form.on('submit(second_dHformStep)', function (data) {
		var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
		var checkStatus = table.checkStatus('tablePLDHSelectId'),checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
		if(checkStatus.isAll && checkData.length!=1){
			easyutils.layMes('error',"不能全选！");
			return false;
		}
        if(checkData.length === 0){
        	easyutils.layMes('error',"请选择数据！");
      		return false;
      	}
	    var newBedUids="",stuNames="";
	    var num = 0;
	    layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){ 
	    	newBedUids+=item.BED_UID+",";
	    	stuNames+=item.STUDENT_NAME+",";
	    	num+=1;
	  	}); 
	    var oldNum = layui.$("#PLDH_OLD_BED_NUMS").val();
		if(parseInt(oldNum) != parseInt(num)){
			easyutils.layMes('error','选择的对换的条数不一致，前者'+oldNum+'条，本次选择'+num+'条');
			return false;
		}
		layui.$("#PLDH_NEW_BED_UIDS").val(newBedUids);
		layui.$("#PLDH_SEL_BSTUDENTS_NAME").val(stuNames);
	    step.next('#dormPlDhStepId');
	    return false;
	  });
	
	  $('.pre').click(function () {
	    step.pre('#dormPlDhStepId');
	  });
	
	  $('.next').click(function () {
	    step.next('#dormPlDhStepId');
	  });

	  //监听提交
	  form.on('submit(finishtz_dHformStep)', function(data){
  	    var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
		field.STUDENT_NAMES='';
		field.STUDENT_NOS='';
		layer.confirm("确认对所选学生的宿舍进行对换保存？", {icon: 3, title:'提示'},
    		function(index){
			easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/stuDormDhManage/saveBedPlDh',field,function successFun(res){
			 	if(res.success){
			 		if(res.resList){
			 			var getTpl = document.getElementById('TPL_pldhdorm_result_init').innerHTML;
			 			var data={resList: res.resList};
			 	    	layui.laytpl(getTpl).render(data, function(html){
			 	    		document.getElementById('pldhdorm_result_id').innerHTML = html;
			 	    	});
	            	}	
			 		step.next('#dormPlDhStepId');
			  	}
		    })
    	    layer.close(index);
	   	});
		
	    
	   //step.next('#stepForm');
		return false;
	  });
	
	  form.on('submit(last_form_pldh)', function(data){
		layui.admin.events.refresh();
	  });
	
	  var selects1=[null,null,null,null];
	  layui.easyutils.selectDormCode('#Q_PLDHS_SELID_STU',selects1,function dormPlDHStuCodeFun(o,d){
			layui.$("#Q_PLDHS_SELVALUE_STU").val(o.values.join(","));
	  });//园区楼宇楼层房间
	  
	  var selcoll=[null,null,null];
	  layui.easyutils.selectCollegeCode('#Q_PLDHS_SELID_COLLEGE',selcoll,function dormPlDHCollCodeFun(o,d){
			layui.$("#Q_PLDHS_SELVALUE_COLLEGE").val(o.values.join(","));
	  });//学院专业班级
	  
	  easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-PLDHS-formlist');
	  form.render(null, 'layadmin-PLDHS-formlist');
	  
	  tableObjPlDHDorms=easytable.init('easy-table-PLDHS',"layadmin-PLDHS-formlist");
	  $("#btn_PLDHSUTID_search").click(function(){
		  easytable.reload(tableObjPlDHDorms,'layadmin-PLDHS-formlist');
	  });
	  
	  $("#btn_PLDHSUTID_reset").click(function(){
		  easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-PLDHS-formlist');
		  form.render(null, 'layadmin-PLDHS-formlist');
	  });
	  
	  //监听行工具事件
	  table.on('tool(easy-table-PLDHS)', function(obj){
	    var data = obj.data;
	    if(obj.event === 'detail'){
	    	var data1 = {bedUid:data.BED_UID};
	    	easyutils.popupViewWindow("查看",'60%','95%','dormstu/dormstu/view','layuiadmin-form-DORMS','easyajax/stuDormManage/getViewMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
	  			//$('#IMG_COVER').attr('src', d.IMG_COVER);
	        });
	    }
	  });
	
	  
    var seldorm=[null,null,null,null];
	layui.easyutils.selectDormCode("#Q_PLDHSelect_SELID_STU",seldorm,function pldhdormStuCodeFun(o,d){
		layui.$("#Q_PLDHSelect_SELVALUE_STU").val(o.values.join(","));
	});//园区楼宇楼层房间
	
	var selcoll1=[null,null,null];
	layui.easyutils.selectCollegeCode('#Q_PLDHSSelect_SELID_COLLEGE',selcoll1,function pldhdormCollCodeFun(o,d){
		layui.$("#Q_PLDHSSelect_SELVALUE_COLLEGE").val(o.values.join(","));
	});//学院专业班级

	easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-PLDHSelect-formlist');
	form.render(null, 'layadmin-PLDHSelect-formlist');
	  
	tableObjPlDHDormSele=layui.easytable.init('easy-table-PLDHSelect',"layadmin-PLDHSelect-formlist");
	
	$("#btn_PLDHSelect_search").click(function(){
	  	easytable.reload(tableObjPlDHDormSele,'layadmin-PLDHSelect-formlist');
	});
	
	$("#btn_PLDHSelect_reset").click(function(){
		var vs = $("#Q_PLDHSelect_ROOM_SEX").val();
		var vs2 = $("#Q_PLDHSelect_BED_UIDS").val();
	  	easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-PLDHSelect-formlist');
	  	form.render(null, 'layadmin-PLDHSelect-formlist');
	  	$("#Q_PLDHSelect_ROOM_SEX").val(vs);
	  	$("#Q_PLDHSelect_BED_UIDS").val(vs2);
    });
	
	
	 //监听行工具事件
	  table.on('tool(easy-table-PLDHSelect)', function(obj){
	    var data = obj.data;
	    if(obj.event === 'detail'){
	    	var data1 = {bedUid:data.BED_UID};
	    	easyutils.popupViewWindow("查看",'60%','95%','dormstu/dormstu/view','layuiadmin-form-DORMS','easyajax/stuDormManage/getViewMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
	  			//$('#IMG_COVER').attr('src', d.IMG_COVER);
	        });
	    }
	  });
	 
	//初始化学年类型
	form.render(null, 'layuiadmin-form-finishtz');
	
});

function dormsPlDHDonFun(res, curr, count){
	layui.tableMerge.render(tableObjPlDHDorms.config,false)
}

function dormSelPlDHDonFun(res, curr, count){
	layui.tableMerge.render(tableObjPlDHDormSele.config,false)
}

<script>
var tableObjPlfpDorms;
var tableObjPlfpDormSele;
layui.use(['easytable','form','laydate','easyutils','tableMerge','step'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,table=layui.table
  ,easytable = layui.easytable
  ,form = layui.form
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils
  ,laydate = layui.laydate
  ,tableMerge = layui.tableMerge
  ,step = layui.step;
  
  
  laydate.render({
    elem: '#DormBedplFp_BEGIN_DATE'
    ,format: 'yyyy-MM-dd'
    ,value: easyutils.getNowFormatDate()
    ,done: function(value, date, endDate){
    }
  });
  
  step.render({
      elem: '#dormPlFpStepId',
      filter: 'dormPlFpStepFilter',
      width: '100%', //设置容器宽度
      stepWidth: '750px',
      height: '1000px',
      stepItems: [{
          title: '查找学生'
      },{
          title: '查找床位'
      },{
          title: '确认分配'
      },{
          title: '完成'
      }]
  });
  
  	form.on('submit(first_formStep)', function (data) {
		var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
		var checkStatus = table.checkStatus('tablePLFPSUTID'),checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
		if(checkStatus.isAll && checkData.length!=1){
			easyutils.layMes('error',"不能全选！");
			return false;
		}
        if(checkData.length === 0){
      		easyutils.layMes('error',"请选择数据！");
      		return false;
      	}
	    var stuUids="",stuNames="",sexCode="",isSame=0;  
	    var num = 0;
	    layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){ 
	    	stuUids+=item.STU_INFO_UID+",";
	    	stuNames+=item.STUDENT_NAME+",";
	    	if(sexCode!=null&&sexCode!=''){
	    		if(sexCode != item.SEX_CODE){
	    			isSame=1;
	    		}
	    	}
	    	sexCode=item.SEX_CODE;
	    	num+=1;
	  	}); 
	    
	    if(isSame==1){
			easyutils.layMes('error',"所选要分配宿舍的学生的性别不一致，请选择同一性别的学生！");
      		return false;
		}
	    
	    layui.$("#PLFP_STU_INFO_UIDS").val(stuUids);
	    layui.$("#PLFP_STUDENT_NAMES").val(stuNames);
	    layui.$("#PLFP_STU_NUMS").val(num);
	    layui.$("#PLFP_SEL_STUDENTS_NAME").val(stuNames);
	    
	    layui.$("#Q_PLFPSelect_ROOM_SEX").val(sexCode);
	    $("#btn_PLDSelect_search").click();
	    
	  	step.next('#dormPlFpStepId');
    	return false;
	});
	
	form.on('submit(second_formStep)', function (data) {
		var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
		var checkStatus = table.checkStatus('tablePLDSelectId'),checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
		if(checkStatus.isAll && checkData.length!=1){
			easyutils.layMes('error',"不能全选！");
			return false;
		}
        if(checkData.length === 0){
        	easyutils.layMes('error',"请选择数据！");
      		return false;
      	}
	    var newBedUids="",newBedNames="";  
	    var num = 0;
	    layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){ 
	    	newBedUids+=item.BED_UID+",";
	    	newBedNames+=item.BED_NAME+",";
	    	num+=1;
	  	}); 
	    var oldNum = layui.$("#PLFP_STU_NUMS").val();
		if(parseInt(oldNum) != parseInt(num)){
			easyutils.layMes('error','选择的床位数和需要分配宿舍的学生数不一致');
			return false;
		}
		layui.$("#PLFP_NEW_BED_UIDS").val(newBedUids);
		layui.$("#PLFP_SEL_BEDS_NAME").val(newBedNames);
		step.next('#dormPlFpStepId');
	    return false;
	});
	
	$('.pre').click(function () {
	    step.pre('#dormPlFpStepId');
	});
	
	$('.next').click(function () {
	    step.next('#dormPlFpStepId');
	});

	//监听提交
	form.on('submit(finishfp_formStep)', function(data){
  	    var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
  	    layer.confirm("确认对所选学生的宿舍的分配信息进行提交保存？", {icon: 3, title:'提示'},
      		function(index){
  	    	easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/stuDormFpManage/saveBedPlFp',field,function successFun(res){
  			 	if(res.success){
  			 		if(res.resList){
  			 			var getTpl = document.getElementById('TPL_plfpdorm_result_init').innerHTML;
  			 			var data={resList: res.resList};
  			 	    	layui.laytpl(getTpl).render(data, function(html){
  			 	    		document.getElementById('plfpdorm_result_id').innerHTML = html;
  			 	    	});
  	            	}
  			 		step.next('#dormPlFpStepId');
  			  	}
  		    })
      	    layer.close(index);
  	   	});
  	    
	    
	   // step.next('#stepForm');
		return false;
	});
	
	form.on('submit(last_form_plfp)', function(data){
		layui.admin.events.refresh();
	});
	
	  var selcoll=[null,null,null];
	  layui.easyutils.selectCollegeCode('#Q_PLFP_SELID_COLLEGE',selcoll,function dormPlfpCollCodeFun(o,d){
			layui.$("#Q_PLFP_SELVALUE_COLLEGE").val(o.values.join(","));
	  });//学院专业班级
	  
	  easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-PLFP-formlist');
	  form.render(null, 'layadmin-PLFP-formlist');
	  
	  tableObjPlfpDorms=easytable.init('easy-table-PLFP',"layadmin-PLFP-formlist");
	  $("#btn_PLFPSUTID_search").click(function(){
		  easytable.reload(tableObjPlfpDorms,'layadmin-PLFP-formlist');
	  });
	  
	  $("#btn_PLFPSUTID_reset").click(function(){
		  easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-PLFP-formlist');
		  form.render(null, 'layadmin-PLFP-formlist');
	  });
	  
	  //监听行工具事件
	  table.on('tool(easy-table-PLFP)', function(obj){
	    var data = obj.data;
	    if(obj.event === 'detail'){
	    	var data1 = {stuInfoUid:data.STU_INFO_UID,isView:"1"};
	    	easyutils.popupViewWindow("学生信息查看",'70%','95%','dormstu/student/view','layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_INFO','easyajax/studentInfoManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
	  			//$('#IMG_COVER').attr('src', d.IMG_COVER);
	        });
	    }
	  });
	
	  
    var selects1=[null,null,null,null];
	layui.easyutils.selectDormCode('#Q_PLFPSelect_SELID_STU',selects1,function plfpdormStuCodeFun(o,d){
		layui.$("#Q_PLFPSelect_SELVALUE_STU").val(o.values.join(","));
	});//园区楼宇楼层房间

	easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-PLFPSelect-formlist');
	form.render(null, 'layadmin-PLFPSelect-formlist');
	  
	tableObjPlfpDormSele=layui.easytable.init('easy-table-PLFPSelect',"layadmin-PLFPSelect-formlist");
	
	$("#btn_PLDSelect_search").click(function(){
	  	easytable.reload(tableObjPlfpDormSele,'layadmin-PLFPSelect-formlist');
	});
	
	$("#btn_PLDSelect_reset").click(function(){
		var vs =$("#Q_PLFPSelect_ROOM_SEX").val();
	  	easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-PLFPSelect-formlist');
	  	form.render(null, 'layadmin-PLFPSelect-formlist');
	  	$("#Q_PLFPSelect_ROOM_SEX").val(vs);
    });
	 
	//初始化学年类型
	form.render(null, 'layuiadmin-form-finishfp');
	
});

function plfpDonFun(res, curr, count){
	layui.tableMerge.render(tableObjPlfpDorms.config,false)
}

function dormSelPlfpDonFun(res, curr, count){
	layui.tableMerge.render(tableObjPlfpDormSele.config,false)
}

<script>
var tableObjPlDorms;
var tableObjPlDormSele;
layui.use(['easytable','form','laydate','easyutils','tableMerge','step'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,table=layui.table
  ,easytable = layui.easytable
  ,form = layui.form
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils
  ,laydate = layui.laydate
  ,tableMerge = layui.tableMerge
  ,step = layui.step;
  
  laydate.render({
    elem: '#DormBedplTz_BEGIN_DATE'
    ,format: 'yyyy-MM-dd'
    ,value: easyutils.getNowFormatDate()
    ,done: function(value, date, endDate){
       
    }
  });
  
    step.render({
      elem: '#dormPlTzStepId',
      filter: 'dormPlTzStepFilter',
      width: '100%', //设置容器宽度
      stepWidth: '750px',
      height: '1000px',
      stepItems: [{
          title: '查找学生'
      },{
          title: '查找床位'
      },{
          title: '确认调整'
      },{
          title: '完成'
      }]
    });
  
  	  form.on('submit(first_formStep)', function (data) {
		var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
		var checkStatus = table.checkStatus('tablePLDSUTID'),checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
// 		if(checkStatus.isAll && checkData.length!=1){
// 			easyutils.layMes('error',"不能全选！");
// 			return false;
// 		}
        if(checkData.length === 0){
      		easyutils.layMes('error',"请选择数据！");
      		return false;
      	}
	    var oldBedUids="",stuUids="",stuNames="",sexCode="",isSame=0;  
	    var num = 0;
	    layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){ 
	    	oldBedUids+=item.BED_UID+",";
	    	stuUids+=item.STU_INFO_UID+",";
	    	stuNames+=item.STUDENT_NAME+",";
	    	if(sexCode!=null&&sexCode!=''){
	    		if(sexCode != item.ROOM_SEX){
	    			isSame=1
	    		}
	    	}
	    	sexCode=item.ROOM_SEX;
	    	num+=1;
	  	}); 
	    
	    if(isSame==1){
	    	easyutils.layMes('error',"所选要调整床位的学生的性别不一致，请选择同一性别的学生！");
      		return false;
		}
	    
	    layui.$("#PLDORM_OLD_BED_UIDS").val(oldBedUids);
	    layui.$("#PLDORM_STU_INFO_UIDS").val(stuUids);
	    layui.$("#PLDORM_SEL_STUDENTS_NAME").val(stuNames);
	    layui.$("#PLDORM_OLD_BED_NUMS").val(num);
	    
	    layui.$("#Q_PLDORMSelect_ROOM_SEX").val(sexCode);
	    $("#btn_PLDSelect_search").click();
	    
	  	step.next('#dormPlTzStepId');
    	return false;
	  });
	
	  form.on('submit(second_formStep)', function (data) {
		var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
		var checkStatus = table.checkStatus('tablePLDSelectId'),checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
// 		if(checkStatus.isAll && checkData.length!=1){
// 			easyutils.layMes('error',"不能全选！");
// 			return false;
// 		}
        if(checkData.length === 0){
        	easyutils.layMes('error',"请选择数据！");
      		return false;
      	}
	    var newBedUids="",bedName="";
	    var num = 0;
	    layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){ 
	    	newBedUids+=item.BED_UID+",";
	    	bedName+=item.BED_NAME+",";
	    	num+=1;
	  	}); 
	    var oldNum = layui.$("#PLDORM_OLD_BED_NUMS").val();
		if(parseInt(oldNum) != parseInt(num)){
			easyutils.layMes('error','选择的床位数和需要调整的学生数不一致');
			return false;
		}
		layui.$("#PLDORM_NEW_BED_UIDS").val(newBedUids);
		layui.$("#PLDORM_SEL_BEDS_NAME").val(bedName);
	    step.next('#dormPlTzStepId');
	    return false;
	  });
	
	  $('.pre').click(function () {
	    step.pre('#dormPlTzStepId');
	  });
	
	  $('.next').click(function () {
	    step.next('#dormPlTzStepId');
	  });

	  //监听提交
	  form.on('submit(finishtz_formStep)', function(data){
  	    var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
  	   // console.log("finish0===",field);
  	    /**
  	    var ov = $("#PLDORM_OLD_MONTHS").val();
		var nv = $("#PLDORM_NEW_MONTHS").val();
		var hv=(ov*1)+(nv*1);//合计值
		if(hv!="10") {
			easyutils.layMes('error','调整宿舍前后入住月数之和等于10个月！');
			return false;
	 	}***/
		field.STUDENT_NAMES='';
		field.STUDENT_NOS='';
		
		layer.confirm("确认对所选学生的宿舍的调整信息进行提交保存？", {icon: 3, title:'提示'},
    		function(index){
			easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/stuDormTzManage/saveBedPlTz',field,function successFun(res){
			 	if(res.success){
			 		if(res.resList){
			 			var getTpl = document.getElementById('TPL_pltzdorm_result_init').innerHTML;
			 			var data={resList: res.resList};
			 	    	layui.laytpl(getTpl).render(data, function(html){
			 	    		document.getElementById('pltzdorm_result_id').innerHTML = html;
			 	    	});
	            	}	
			 		step.next('#dormPlTzStepId');
			  	}
		    })
    	    layer.close(index);
	   	});
		
	    
	   // step.next('#stepForm');
		return false;
	  });
	
	  form.on('submit(last_form_pltz)', function(data){
		layui.admin.events.refresh();
	  });
	
	  var selects1=[null,null,null,null];
	  layui.easyutils.selectDormCode('#Q_PLDORMS_SELID_STU',selects1,function dormPlStuCodeFun(o,d){

	  });//学院专业班级
	  
	  easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-PLDORMS-formlist');
	  form.render(null, 'layadmin-PLDORMS-formlist');
	  
	  tableObjPlDorms=easytable.init('easy-table-PLDORMS',"layadmin-PLDORMS-formlist");
	  $("#btn_PLDSUTID_search").click(function(){

	  });

	  table.on('tool(easy-table-PLDORMS)', function(obj){

	    }

    });
	 
	//初始化学年类型
	form.render(null, 'layuiadmin-form-finishtz');

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils','laytpl'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,form = layui.form
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils
  ,laytpl = layui.laytpl;
 
  easyutils.renderDateYear('layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE',1);
  
	 //监听提交
     form.on('submit(LAY-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE-submit)', function(data){
       	var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
       	layer.confirm('确定修改该数据至收费系统？此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
       		easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/stuBedfeeManage/updateBedFee',field,function successFun(res){
      			if(res.success){
      				$("#btn_bedfeeUid_search").click();//刷新
      				$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
        		}
      		});
   		});
     });
     
     $("#btn_DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE_close").click(function(){
    	 $("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
     });
     
     $("#btn_bfree").click(function(){
    		var stuData = $("#btn_bfree_STUDENT_NO").val();
    		if(stuData!=null && stuData!=''){
    			var data1 = {stuNo:stuData};
    	  	  	easyutils.reqGet('easyajax/stuBedfeeManage/getBedFeeMap',data1,function successFun(res){
    	  	  		if(res.success){
    	  	  			var successData=res.data;
	    	  	 		var getTpl = document.getElementById('TPL_cwfyzsfjl_value').innerHTML;
	    	  	 		laytpl(getTpl).render(successData, function(html){
	    	  	 			document.getElementById('cwfyzsfjl').innerHTML  = "";
	    	  	 			document.getElementById('cwfyzsfjl').innerHTML = html;
	    	  	 		});
	    	  	 		
	    	  	 		getTpl = document.getElementById('TPL_cwxtxsfyjl_value').innerHTML;
	    	  	 		laytpl(getTpl).render(successData, function(html){
	    	  	 			console.log(html);
	    	  	 			document.getElementById('cwxtxsfyjl').innerHTML = "";
	    	  	 			document.getElementById('cwxtxsfyjl').innerHTML = html;
	    	  	 		});
	    	  	 		
    	  		    }else{
    	  		        easyutils.layMes('error',res.reasonremark);
  	   		    		return false;
    	  		    }
    	  		}); 
    		}else{
    			easyutils.layMes('error','请输入学号！');
   		    return false;
    		}
      });
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,form = layui.form
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
 
  easyutils.renderDateYear('layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE',1);
  
	 //监听提交
     form.on('submit(LAY-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE-submit)', function(data){
       	var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
       	layer.confirm('确定修改该数据至收费系统？此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
       		easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/stuBedfeeManage/updateBedFee',field,function successFun(res){
      			if(res.success){
      				$("#btn_bedfeeUid_search").click();//刷新
      				$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
        		}
      		});
   		});
     });
     
     $("#btn_DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE_close").click(function(){
    	 $("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
     });
     
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,table=layui.table
  ,easytable = layui.easytable
  ,form = layui.form
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils;

  easyutils.renderDateYear('layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE-formlist',1);
  
  var selects1=[null,null,null];
  layui.easyutils.selectCollegeCode('#Q_BEDFEE_SELID_COLLEGE',selects1,function bedFeeCodeFun(o,d){
		layui.$("#Q_BEDFEE_SELVALUE_COLLEGE").val(o.values.join(","));
  });//学院专业班级
  
  easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE-formlist');
  form.render(null, 'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE-formlist');
  
  var tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE',"layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE-formlist");
  $("#btn_bedfeeUid_search").click(function(){
	  easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE-formlist');
  });
  
  $("#btn_bedfeeUid_reset").click(function(){
	  easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE-formlist');
	  form.render(null, 'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE-formlist');
  });
  
  //头工具栏事件
  table.on('toolbar(easy-table-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE)', function(obj){
    switch(obj.event){
      case 'stu_bedfee':
	      layer.confirm('确定生成学年的学生住宿费用明细数据？此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
	           easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/stuBedfeeManage/initBedFee',null,function successFun(res){
	   	  			if(res.success){
	   	  				$("#btn_bedfeeUid_search").click(); //刷新
	   	    		}
	   	  		});
      		});
      break;
      case 'updateToCw':
    	  easyutils.popupWindow("更新学生宿舍费用",'60%','95%','dormstu/bedfee/bedfee_input','layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE',null,null,function renderDoneFun(d){
        		
          });
      break;
    };
  });
  
  //监听行工具事件
  table.on('tool(easy-table-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE)', function(obj){
    var data = obj.data;
    if(obj.event === 'edit'){
      	var data1 = {bedfeeUid:data.BEDFEE_UID,isView:'0'};
      	easyutils.popupWindow("编辑",'80%','95%','dormstu/bedfee/input','layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE','easyajax/stuBedfeeManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
      		easyutils.val('layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE',d);
        });    
    } else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
    	var data1 = {bedfeeUid:data.BEDFEE_UID,isView:'1'};
    	easyutils.popupViewWindow("查看",'80%','95%','dormstu/bedfee/view','layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE','easyajax/stuBedfeeManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
  			
        });
    }
  });

});
</script>

</style>

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,table=layui.table
  ,easytable = layui.easytable
  ,form = layui.form
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
  
  easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_RETURN-formlist');
  form.render(null, 'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_RETURN-formlist');
  

//监听提交
  form.on('submit(layuiadmin-form-DORM_CHANGE)', function(data){
    	var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
    	easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/stuDormDhManage/save',field,function successFun(res){
			if(res.success){
				
 			}
		});
  });
  
  
  $("#btn_search_change_one").click(function(){
 		var stuData = $("#SEARCH_STU_DATA_CHANGE_ONE").val();
 		if(stuData!=null && stuData!=''){
 			var data1 = {SEARCH_STU_DATA:stuData};
 	  	  	easyutils.reqGet('easyajax/stuDormManage/getStuDormMap',data1,function successFun(res){
 	  	  		if(res.success){
 	  	  			var successData=res.data;
 	  	  			easyutils.val("layuiadmin-form-DORM_CHANGE_ONE",successData);
 	  	  			$("#ONE_BED_UID").val(successData.BED_UID);
 	  		    }else{
 	  		        easyutils.layMes('error',res.reasonremark);
	   		    	return false;
 	  		    }
 	  		}); 
 		}else{
 			easyutils.layMes('error','请输入学号/身份证号！');
		    return false;
 		}
   });
  
  
  $("#btn_search_change_two").click(function(){
		var stuData = $("#SEARCH_STU_DATA_CHANGE_TWO").val();
		if(stuData!=null && stuData!=''){
			var data1 = {SEARCH_STU_DATA:stuData};
	  	  	easyutils.reqGet('easyajax/stuDormManage/getStuDormMap',data1,function successFun(res){
	  	  		if(res.success){
	  	  			var successData=res.data;
	  	  			easyutils.val("layuiadmin-form-DORM_CHANGE_TWO",successData);
	  	  			$("#TWO_BED_UID").val(successData.BED_UID);
	  		    }else{
	  		        easyutils.layMes('error',res.reasonremark);
	   		    	return false;
	  		    }
	  		}); 
		}else{
			easyutils.layMes('error','请输入学号/身份证号！');
		    return false;
		}
 });

});

</script>

<style>
.layui-upload-img{width: 92px; height: 92px; margin: 0 10px 10px 0;}
</style>

<div class="layui-form layui-form-pane" lay-filter="layuiadmin-form-DORMS" >
  <fieldset class="layui-elem-field ">
     <legend style="color:#393D49;">床位详情信息</legend>

<script>
layui.use(['form','laytpl','easyutils','laydate','easyUpload'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,form = layui.form
  ,laytpl = layui.laytpl
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils
  ,laydate = layui.laydate
  ,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
  
  
  	laydate.render({
	    elem: '#U_ONE_YEAR_NUM'
	    ,format: 'yyyy-MM-dd'
	    ,value: easyutils.getNowFormatDate()
	    ,done: function(value, date, endDate){
	    	layui.$("#U_ONE_PARAM0").val(layui.$("#U_ONE_YEAR_NUM").val());
	    }
	});
  
  
//初始化上传控件界面
  easyUpload.initClickFileUploadHtml(null,function successFun(res){
		var data={num:0,title:'学生住宿文件上传'};
    	layui.laytpl(res.innerHTML).render(data, function(html){
    		document.getElementById('uploadStuBedFileId0').innerHTML = html;
    		layui.$("#U_ONE_PARAM0").val(easyutils.getNowFormatDate());
    	});
   });
  //初始化上传控件
  easyUpload.initClickFileUpload(0,'easyfile/stuDormManage/importStuBedExcel',function successFun(res){
		if(res.success){
			$("#down_mes_0").html(res.resultinfo);
			$("#imp_retfilepath_0").val(res.retfilepath);
			$("#resultinfoId_0").show();
			$("#btn_DSUTID_search").click(); //刷新
   		}
  });

  //导出结果下载
  $("#downResButton0").click(function(){
	  var f = $("#imp_retfilepath_0").val();
	  if(f!=null && f!=''){
		  easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/uploadManage/downResult?fileName='+f,'impstubed_result');
	  }else{
		  easyutils.layMes('error',"下载文件不存在！");
	  }
  });
  
  $("#downButton").click(function(){
	  easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/uploadManage/downTemplate?fileName=imp_stu_bed.xlsx','impStuBed');
  });
  
});

</script>

<script>
var tableObjDormSele;

layui.use(['admin', 'form','laydate','easytable','easyutils','tableMerge','step'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,table=layui.table
  ,easytable = layui.easytable
  ,form = layui.form
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils
  ,laydate = layui.laydate
  ,tableMerge = layui.tableMerge
  ,step = layui.step;
  
  laydate.render({
    elem: '#DormBedTz_BEGIN_DATE'
    ,format: 'yyyy-MM-dd'
    ,value: easyutils.getNowFormatDate()
    ,done: function(value, date, endDate){
       
    }
  });
  
  step.render({
      elem: '#dormTzStepId',
      filter: 'dormTzStepFilter',
      width: '100%', //设置容器宽度
      stepWidth: '750px',
      height: '800px',
      stepItems: [{

      }, {

      }]
  });
  
    form.render(null, 'layuiadmin-form-finish');

	layui.easyutils.selectDormCode('#Q_DORMSelect_SELID_STU',seldormtz,function dormTzStuCodeFun(o,d){

	});//园区楼宇楼层房间

	easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-DORMSelect-formlist');
	form.render(null, 'layadmin-DORMSelect-formlist');

	});
	
	$("#btn_DSelect_reset").click(function(){
		var vs = $("#Q_DORMSelect_ROOM_SEX").val();
	  	easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-DORMSelect-formlist');
	  	form.render(null, 'layadmin-DORMSelect-formlist');
	  	$("#Q_DORMSelect_ROOM_SEX").val(vs);
    });
  
  
	//监听行工具事件
    table.on('tool(easy-table-DORMSelect)', function(obj){
      	var data = obj.data;
      	if(obj.event === 'selectObj'){
        	$("#DormBedTz_NEW_BED_UID").val(data.BED_UID);
        	var roobed=data.GARDEN_NAME+data.BUILDING_NAME+"栋"+data.ROOM_NAME+"房间"+data.BED_NAME+"号床";
        	$("#NEW_DORM_ROOM_BED").val(roobed);
        	//下一步
        	step.next('#dormTzStepId');
        	return false;
      	}
    });

    $('#DORM_OLD_MONTHS').change(function() {
    	var dxn = $('input[name="DORM_TZXN"]:checked').val();

    		$("#DORM_OLD_MONTHS").val(0);
    		$("#DORM_NEW_MONTHS").val(10);

        		$("#DORM_OLD_MONTHS").val(10)
        		$("#DORM_NEW_MONTHS").val(0);

		}

  form.on('submit(first_formStep)', function (data) {
		var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
  		//console.log("first",field);
	  	var nbid = $("#DormBedTz_NEW_BED_UID").val();
		if(nbid!='' && nbid!=null){
			step.next('#dormTzStepId');
		}else{
			easyutils.layMes('error',"请回到上一步，查找空床位！");
			return false;
		}
      	return false;
  });

  form.on('submit(second_formStep)', function (data) {
	  var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
  	//  console.log("second",field);
      step.next('#dormTzStepId');
      return false;
  });

  $('.pre').click(function () {
      step.pre('#dormTzStepId');
  });

  $('.next').click(function () {
      step.next('#dormTzStepId');
  });
  
  //监听提交
  form.on('submit(finish_formStep)', function(data){
    	var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
    	//console.log("finish0===",field);
    	/**
    	var ov = $("#DORM_OLD_MONTHS").val();
		var nv = $("#DORM_NEW_MONTHS").val();
		var hv=(ov*1)+(nv*1);//合计值
 		if(hv!="10") {
 			easyutils.layMes('error',"调整宿舍前后入住月数之和等于10个月！");
 			return false;
	 	}**/
 		//console.log("finish===",field);
		var nbid = $("#DormBedTz_NEW_BED_UID").val();
		if(nbid!='' && nbid!=null){
			layer.confirm("确认对所选学生的宿舍的调整信息进行提交保存？", {icon: 3, title:'提示'},
		    	function(index){
					easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/stuDormTzManage/saveBedTz',field,function successFun(res){
			 			if(res.success){
			 				if(res.resList){
					 			var getTpl = document.getElementById('TPL_pltzdorm_result_init').innerHTML;
					 			var data={resList: res.resList};
					 	    	layui.laytpl(getTpl).render(data, function(html){
					 	    		document.getElementById('pltzdorm_result_id').innerHTML = html;
					 	    	});
			            	}
			 				$("#btn_DSUTID_search").click();
			 				//下一步
			 	        	step.next('#dormTzStepId');
			 				//$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗			
			  			}
		 			})	
		    	layer.close(index);
		   	});
			
			
		}else{
			easyutils.layMes('error',"请回到上一步，查找空床位！");
			return false;
		}
		return false;
	});
  
});

}

	layui.tableMerge.render(tableObjDormSele.config,false)

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils','laydate'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,form = layui.form
  ,laydate=layui.laydate
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
  
  
  easyutils.render(null,'layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_RETURN');
	laydate.render({
	    elem: '#DormBedTs_END_DATE'
	    ,format: 'yyyy-MM-dd'
	    ,value: easyutils.getNowFormatDate()
	    ,done: function(value, date, endDate){
	       
	    }
	});

	
	 //监听提交
     form.on('submit(LAY-DORM_STUDENT_RETURN-submit)', function(data){
       	var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
       	layer.confirm("确定直接对该学生不做二次审核直接退宿吗？此操作不能撤销！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'},
     		function(index){
	       		easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/stuReturnManage/saveAudit',field,function successFun(res){
	      			if(res.success){
	      				$("#btn_returnUid_search").click();//刷新
	      				$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
	        		}
	      		});
     	   	layer.close(index);
     	});
     });
     
     $("#btn_DORM_STUDENT_RETURN_close").click(function(){
    	 $("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
     });
     
     
     $("#btn_search_retDorm").click(function(){
   		var stuData = $("#SEARCH_STU_DATA_retDorm_ID").val();
   		if(stuData!=null && stuData!=''){
   			var data1 = {SEARCH_STU_DATA:stuData};
   	  	  	easyutils.reqGet('easyajax/stuDormManage/getStuDormMap',data1,function successFun(res){
   	  	  		if(res.success){
   	  	  			var successData=res.data;
   	  	  			easyutils.val("layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_RETURN",successData);
   	  	  			$("#retDorm-STU_INFO_UID").val(successData.STU_INFO_UID);
   	  	  			$("#retDorm-STUDENT_NO").val(successData.STUDENT_NO);
   	  	  			$("#retDorm-BED_UID").val(successData.BED_UID);
   	  		    }else{
   	  		        easyutils.layMes('error',res.reasonremark);
 	   		    	return false;
   	  		    }
   	  		}); 
   		}else{
   			easyutils.layMes('error','请输入学号/身份证号！');
  		    return false;
   		}
     });
   	
   	$(document).keydown(function (e) {
 		if (e.keyCode === 13) {
 		  	$("#btn_search_retDorm").trigger("click");
 		}
 	});
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils','laydate'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,form = layui.form
  ,laydate = layui.laydate
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
   
  easyutils.render(null,'layuiadmin-form-DORM_RETURNAUDIT');
  	laydate.render({
	    elem: '#DormBedTs_END_DATE'
	    ,format: 'yyyy-MM-dd'
	    ,value: easyutils.getNowFormatDate()
	    ,done: function(value, date, endDate){
	       
	    }
	});
  
  	form.on('submit(LAY-DORM_RETURNAUDIT-submit)', function(data){
       	var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
       	layer.confirm('对该生的退宿信息进行审核确认保存？',{ 
       		btn:['确认','取消'],
       		success:function(){
       			console.log("success:function");
       			this.enterEsc = function (event) {
       				if (event.keyCode === 13) {
       					easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/stuReturnManage/audit',field,function successFun(res){
       		      			if(res.success){
       		      				$("#btn_retAuditUid_search").click();//刷新
       		      				layer.closeAll('dialog');
       		      				$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
       		        		}
       		      		})
       					return false; //阻止系统默认回车事件
       				}else if(event.keyCode == 27){
       					console.log("=============================27")	
       					return false; 
       				}
       			};
       			$(document).on('keydown', this.enterEsc); //监听键盘事件，关闭层
       		},
       		end:function(){
       			$(document).off('keydown',this.enterEsc); //解除键盘关闭事件
       		}
       	},
       	function (index) {//点击确定后执行的方法体
       		console.log(index);
       		easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/stuReturnManage/audit',field,function successFun(res){
      			if(res.success){
      				$("#btn_retAuditUid_search").click();//刷新
      				$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
        		}
      		});
       		layer.close(index);    //执行完后关闭
       	});
     });
  	
  	
	 //监听提交
	 /***
     form.on('submit(LAY-DORM_RETURNAUDIT-submit)', function(data){

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils','laydate','easyUpload'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,table=layui.table
  ,easytable = layui.easytable
  ,form = layui.form
  ,laydate = layui.laydate
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils
  ,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
  
  laydate.render({
    elem: '#D_RETURNAUDIT_TIME_0'
    ,format: 'yyyy-MM-dd'
  });
  
  laydate.render({
    elem: '#D_RETURNAUDIT_TIME_1'
    ,format: 'yyyy-MM-dd'
  });
	  
  easyutils.renderDateYear('layadmin-DORM_RETURNAUDIT-formlist');
  
  var seldorm=[null,null,null,null];
  layui.easyutils.selectDormCode('#Q_RETURNAUDIT_SELID_STU',seldorm,function returnAuditStuCodeFun(o,d){
		layui.$("#Q_RETURNAUDIT_SELVALUE_STU").val(o.values.join(","));
  });//园区楼宇楼层房间
  
  var selcoll=[null,null,null];
  layui.easyutils.selectCollegeCode('#Q_RETURNAUDIT_SELID_COLLEGE',selcoll,function returnAuditCollCodeFun(o,d){
		layui.$("#Q_RETURNAUDIT_SELVALUE_COLLEGE").val(o.values.join(","));
  });//学院专业班级
  
  easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-DORM_RETURNAUDIT-formlist');
  form.render(null, 'layadmin-DORM_RETURNAUDIT-formlist');
  
  var tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-DORM_RETURNAUDIT',"layadmin-DORM_RETURNAUDIT-formlist");
  $("#btn_retAuditUid_search").click(function(){
	  $("#DORM_RETURN_ISE").val("0");
	  easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-DORM_RETURNAUDIT-formlist');
  });
  
  $("#btn_retAuditUid_reset").click(function(){
	  easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-DORM_RETURNAUDIT-formlist');
	  form.render(null, 'layadmin-DORM_RETURNAUDIT-formlist');
	  $("#DORM_RETURN_ISE").val("0");
  });
  
//头工具栏事件
  table.on('toolbar(easy-table-DORM_RETURNAUDIT)', function(obj){
    switch(obj.event){
      case 'batchaudit':
    	  var checkStatus = table.checkStatus(obj.config.id) 
        	  ,checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
	      if(checkData.length === 0){
	      	  return layer.msg('请选择数据');
	      }
	      var checkUids="" ,isCon=true;  
  	      var checkNames = [],checkNos=[],checkAddress=[];
  	      layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){ 
  	    	 if(item.RETURN_STATUS!='0'){
  	  			layer.msg('所选择数据包括非待审数据，请核实之后再进行批量审核！');
  	  			isCon=false;
  	  		 }
  	    	 checkUids+=item.RETURN_UID+",";
  	  		 checkNames.push(item.STUDENT_NAME);
  	  		 checkNos.push(item.STUDENT_NO);
  	  		 var add = item.GARDEN_NAME+item.BUILDING_NAME+'栋'+item.ROOM_NAME+ '房()'+item.ROOMTYPE_MONEY+')';
  	  		 checkAddress.push(add);
  	  	  }); 
  	      if(isCon){
  	    	  var data1 = {checkNames:checkNames,checkNos:checkNos,checkAddress:checkAddress};
    	      easyutils.popupDataWindow("退宿批量审核",'90%','95%','dormstu/returnaudit/bataudit_input','layuiadmin-form-DORM_RETURNAUDIT',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
    	    	  $("#retDorm-RETURN_UIDS").val(checkUids);
    	      });
  	      }
  	      
      break;
      case 'return_export':
    	  layer.confirm("确定导出全部数据吗？数据过大时，请使用查询条件进行筛选过滤！", {icon: 3, title:'提示'},
  	    	function(index){
  	    		  $("#DORM_RETURN_ISE").val("1");
  	    		  var formatjson=easytable.queryWhereFun('layadmin-DORM_RETURNAUDIT-formlist');
  	    	      var dataP = 'conditions='+formatjson.conditions+'&otherConditions='+formatjson.otherConditions;
  	    	      easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/stuReturnManage/query',"退宿名单.xlsx",dataP);
  	    	      $("#DORM_RETURN_ISE").val("0");
  	    	      layer.close(index);
  	   	 	});
      break;
    };
  });
  
  //监听行工具事件
  table.on('tool(easy-table-DORM_RETURNAUDIT)', function(obj){
    var data = obj.data;
    if(obj.event === 'editaudit'){
      	var data1 = {returnUid:data.RETURN_UID};
      	easyutils.popupViewWindow("审核",'70%','95%','dormstu/returnaudit/audit_input','layuiadmin-form-DORM_RETURNAUDIT','easyajax/stuReturnManage/getViewMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
      		$("#retDorm-RETURN_UID").val(d.RETURN_UID);
        });    
    }else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
    	var data1 = {returnUid:data.RETURN_UID};
    	easyutils.popupViewWindow("查看",'60%','95%','dormstu/return/view','layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_RETURN','easyajax/stuReturnManage/getViewMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
        });
    }else if(obj.event === 'edit'){
      	var data1 = {stuNo:data.STUDENT_NO,isView:'0'};
      	easyutils.popupWindow("修改住宿费用",'80%','95%','dormstu/bedfee/bedfee_input','layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE','easyajax/stuBedfeeManage/getBedFeeMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
      		easyutils.val('layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE',d);
        });    
    } 
  });

});

</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils','laydate'], function(){
	  var $ = layui.$
	  ,form = layui.form
	  ,laydate = layui.laydate
	  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
	   
	  easyutils.render(null,'layuiadmin-form-DORM_RETURNAUDIT');
	  	laydate.render({
		    elem: '#DormBedTs_END_DATE'
		    ,format: 'yyyy-MM-dd'
		    ,value: easyutils.getNowFormatDate()
		    ,done: function(value, date, endDate){
		       
		    }
		});
	  
	  	form.on('submit(LAY-DORM_RETURNAUDIT-submit)', function(data){
	       	var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
	       	layer.confirm('对所选学生的退宿信息进行批量审核确认保存？',{ 
	       		btn:['确认','取消'],
	       		success:function(){
	       			console.log("success:function");
	       			this.enterEsc = function (event) {
	       				if (event.keyCode === 13) {
	       					easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/stuReturnManage/batAudit',field,function successFun(res){
	       		      			if(res.success){
	       		      				$("#btn_retAuditUid_search").click();//刷新
	       		      				layer.closeAll('dialog');
	       		      				$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
	       		        		}
	       		      		})
	       					return false; //阻止系统默认回车事件
	       				}else if(event.keyCode == 27){
	       					console.log("=============================27")	
	       					return false; 
	       				}
	       			};
	       			$(document).on('keydown', this.enterEsc); //监听键盘事件，关闭层
	       		},
	       		end:function(){
	       			$(document).off('keydown',this.enterEsc); //解除键盘关闭事件
	       		}
	       	},
	       	function (index) {//点击确定后执行的方法体
	       		easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/stuReturnManage/batAudit',field,function successFun(res){
	      			if(res.success){
	      				$("#btn_retAuditUid_search").click();//刷新
	      				$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
	        		}
	      		});
	       		layer.close(index);    //执行完后关闭
	       	});
	     });

	     $("#btn_DORM_RETURN_close").click(function(){
	    	 $("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
	     });
	     
	});
</script>

<script>
var tableObjTsDorms;
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils','laydate','tableMerge'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,table=layui.table
  ,easytable = layui.easytable
  ,form = layui.form
  ,tableMerge = layui.tableMerge
  ,laydate = layui.laydate
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
  
 
  
  var seldorm=[null,null,null,null];
  layui.easyutils.selectDormCode('#Q_batRETURN_SELID_STU',seldorm,function breturnStuCodeFun(o,d){
		layui.$("#Q_batRETURN_SELVALUE_STU").val(o.values.join(","));
  });//园区楼宇楼层房间
  
  var selcoll=[null,null,null];
  layui.easyutils.selectCollegeCode('#Q_batRETURN_SELID_COLLEGE',selcoll,function breturnCollCodeFun(o,d){
		layui.$("#Q_batRETURN_SELVALUE_COLLEGE").val(o.values.join(","));
  });//学院专业班级
  
  easyutils.renderDateYear('layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_batRETURN-formlist');
  easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_batRETURN-formlist');
  form.render(null, 'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_batRETURN-formlist');
  
  tableObjTsDorms=easytable.init('easy-table-DORM_STUDENT_batRETURN',"layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_batRETURN-formlist");
  $("#btn_batRETURNUid_search").click(function(){
	  easytable.reload(tableObjTsDorms,'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_batRETURN-formlist');
  });
  
  $("#btn_batRETURNUid_reset").click(function(){
	  easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_batRETURN-formlist');
	  form.render(null, 'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_batRETURN-formlist');
  });
  
//头工具栏事件
  table.on('toolbar(easy-table-DORM_STUDENT_batRETURN)', function(obj){
    switch(obj.event){
      case 'batchreturn':
    	var checkStatus = table.checkStatus(obj.config.id) 
      	,checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
	      if(checkData.length === 0){
	      	return layer.msg('请选择数据');
	      }
	      var checkUids="" ,isCon=true;   
	      var checkNames = [],checkNos=[];
	      layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){ 
	  		checkUids+=item.BED_UID+",";
	  		checkNames.push(item.STUDENT_NAME);
  	  		checkNos.push(item.STUDENT_NO);
	  		if(item.BED_STATUS!='2'){
  	  			layer.msg('所选择数据包括非已住的数据，请核实之后再进行批量退宿操作！');
  	  			isCon=false;
  	  		}
	  	  }); 
	      if(isCon){
	    	  var data1 = {checkNames:checkNames,checkNos:checkNos};
	  	      easyutils.popupDataWindow("批量退宿",'80%','95%','dormstu/returnbatch/bat_input','layuiadmin-form-batRETURN',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
	  	    	  $("#batreturn_bedUids").val(checkUids);
	  	      });
	      }
	      
      break;
      case 'impreturn':
    	  easyutils.popupDataWindow("学生退宿数据导入",'60%','95%','dormstu/returnbatch/return_import','layuiadmin-form-batRETURN_IMP',null,function renderDoneFun(d){
          	
          });
      break;
    };
  });
  
//监听行工具事件
  table.on('tool(easy-table-DORM_STUDENT_batRETURN)', function(obj){
    var data = obj.data;
    if(obj.event === 'detailDorm'){
    	var data1 = {bedUid:data.BED_UID};
    	easyutils.popupViewWindow("查看",'60%','95%','dormstu/dormstu/view','layuiadmin-form-DORMS','easyajax/stuDormManage/getViewMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
  			//$('#IMG_COVER').attr('src', d.IMG_COVER);
        });
    }
  });
});


function dormsTsDonFun(res, curr, count){
	layui.tableMerge.render(tableObjTsDorms.config,false)
}

</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','laytpl','easyutils','laydate','easyUpload'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,form = layui.form
  ,laytpl = layui.laytpl
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils
  ,laydate = layui.laydate
  ,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
  
  
	laydate.render({
	    elem: '#U_ONE_YEAR_NUM'
	    ,format: 'yyyy-MM-dd'
	    ,value: easyutils.getNowFormatDate()
	    ,done: function(value, date, endDate){
	    	layui.$("#U_ONE_PARAM0").val(layui.$("#U_ONE_YEAR_NUM").val());
	    	layui.$("#U_TWO_PARAM0").val(layui.$("input[name='RETURN_TYPE']:checked").val());
	    }
	});
  
//初始化上传控件界面
  easyUpload.initClickFileUploadHtml(null,function successFun(res){
		var data={num:0,title:'学生批量退宿数据上传'};
    	layui.laytpl(res.innerHTML).render(data, function(html){
    		document.getElementById('uploadStuBedRetFileId0').innerHTML = html;
    		layui.$("#U_ONE_PARAM0").val(easyutils.getNowFormatDate());
    		layui.$("#U_TWO_PARAM0").val(layui.$("input[name='RETURN_TYPE']:checked").val());
    	});
   });
  //初始化上传控件
  easyUpload.initClickFileUpload(0,'easyfile/stuReturnManage/importExcel',function successFun(res){
		if(res.success){
			$("#down_mes_0").html(res.resultinfo);
			$("#imp_retfilepath_0").val(res.retfilepath);
			$("#resultinfoId_0").show();
			$("#btn_batRETURNUid_search").click(); //刷新
   		}
  });

  //导出结果下载
  $("#downResButton0").click(function(){
	  var f = $("#imp_retfilepath_0").val();
	  if(f!=null && f!=''){
		  easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/uploadManage/downResult?fileName='+f,'impbatchreturn_result');
	  }else{
		  easyutils.layMes('error',"下载文件不存在！");
	  }
  });
  
  $("#downButton").click(function(){
	  easyUpload.downloadData(layui.setter.apiUrl()+'easyfile/uploadManage/downTemplate?fileName=imp_batchreturn.xlsx','imp_batchreturn');
  });
  
  
  form.on('radio(lay_imp_RETURN_TYPE)', function(data){
	  layui.$("#U_ONE_PARAM0").val(layui.$("#U_ONE_YEAR_NUM").val());
	  layui.$("#U_TWO_PARAM0").val(data.value);
	  layui.$("#U_THREE_PARAM0").val(layui.$("#U_ONE_RETURN_REMARK").val());
  });
  
});

function remarkOnblurFun(){
	layui.$("#U_ONE_PARAM0").val(layui.$("#U_ONE_YEAR_NUM").val());
	layui.$("#U_TWO_PARAM0").val(layui.$("input[name='RETURN_TYPE']:checked").val());
	layui.$("#U_THREE_PARAM0").val(layui.$("#U_ONE_RETURN_REMARK").val());
}
</script>

<script>
var tableObjDormLb;
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils','tableMerge','easyUpload'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,table=layui.table
  ,easytable = layui.easytable
  ,form = layui.form
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils
  ,tableMerge = layui.tableMerge
  ,easyUpload=layui.easyUpload;
  
  
  var seldorm=[null,null,null,null];
  layui.easyutils.selectDormCode('#Q_DORMLB_SELID_STU',seldorm,function dormStuCodeFun(o,d){
		layui.$("#Q_DORMLB_SELVALUE_STU").val(o.values.join(","));
  });//园区楼宇楼层房间
  
  var selcoll=[null,null,null];
  layui.easyutils.selectCollegeCode('#Q_DORMLB_SELID_COLLEGE',selcoll,function dormCollCodeFun(o,d){
		layui.$("#Q_DORMLB_SELVALUE_COLLEGE").val(o.values.join(","));
  });//学院专业班级
  
  easyutils.renderDateYear('layadmin-DORMLB-formlist');
  easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-DORMLB-formlist');
  form.render(null, 'layadmin-DORMLB-formlist');
  
  tableObjDormLb=easytable.init('easy-table-DORMLB',"layadmin-DORMLB-formlist");
  $("#btn_DORMLB_search").click(function(){
	  easytable.reload(tableObjDormLb,'layadmin-DORMLB-formlist');
  });
  
  $("#btn_DORMLB_reset").click(function(){
	  easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-DORMLB-formlist');
	  form.render(null, 'layadmin-DORMLB-formlist');
  });

  
  //监听行工具事件
  table.on('tool(easy-table-DORMLB)', function(obj){
    var data = obj.data;
    if(obj.event === 'detail'){
    	var data1 = {bedUid:data.BED_UID};
    	easyutils.popupViewWindow("住宿情况查看",'60%','95%','dormstu/dormstu/view','layuiadmin-form-DORMS','easyajax/stuDormManage/getViewMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
  			//$('#IMG_COVER').attr('src', d.IMG_COVER);
        });
    }else if(obj.event === 'detailStu'){
    	var data1 = {stuInfoUid:data.STU_INFO_UID,isView:"1"};
    	easyutils.popupViewWindow("学生信息查看",'70%','95%','dormstu/student/view','layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_INFO','easyajax/studentInfoManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
  			
        });
    }
  });

});

function dormsDonlBFun(res, curr, count){
	layui.tableMerge.render(tableObjDormLb.config,false)
}
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,form = layui.form
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
   
	 //监听提交
     form.on('submit(LAY-DORM_STUDENT_INFO-submit)', function(data){
       	var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
       	easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/studentInfoManage/saveOrUpdate',field,function successFun(res){
  			if(res.success){
  				$("#btn_stuInfoUid_search").click();//刷新
  				$("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
    		}
  		});
     });
     
     $("#btn_DORM_STUDENT_INFO_close").click(function(){
    	 $("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
     });
     
});
</script>

<script>
layui.use(['easytable','easyutils'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,table=layui.table
  ,easytable = layui.easytable
  ,form = layui.form
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
  
  easyutils.renderDateYear('layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_INFO-formlist');
  easyutils.render(null,'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_INFO-formlist');
  form.render(null, 'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_INFO-formlist');

  var selects1=[null,null,null];
  layui.easyutils.selectCollegeCode('#Q_DORMSTU_SELID_COLLEGE',selects1,function dormStuCodeFun(o,d){
		layui.$("#Q_DORMSTU_SELVALUE_COLLEGE").val(o.values.join(","));
  });//学院专业班级
  
  var tableObj=easytable.init('easy-table-DORM_STUDENT_INFO',"layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_INFO-formlist");
  $("#btn_stuInfoUid_search").click(function(){
	  easytable.reload(tableObj,'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_INFO-formlist');
  });
  
  $("#btn_stuInfoUid_reset").click(function(){
	  easyutils.resetVal('layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_INFO-formlist');
	  form.render(null, 'layadmin-DORM_STUDENT_INFO-formlist');
  });
  
//头工具栏事件
  table.on('toolbar(easy-table-DORM_STUDENT_INFO)', function(obj){
    switch(obj.event){
      case 'syn_stu':
    	  easyutils.popupDataWindow("从迎新系统同步",'50%','95%','dormstu/student/syn_stu','layuiadmin-form-STU_SYN',null,function renderDoneFun(d){
          	
          });
      break;
      case 'syn_one':
    	  easyutils.popupDataWindow("单个学生同步",'50%','95%','dormstu/student/syn_one','layuiadmin-form-STU_ONE',null,function renderDoneFun(d){
          	
          });
      break;
      case 'syn_onestuinfo':
    	  easyutils.popupDataWindow("学籍单个学生获取",'50%','95%','dormstu/student/syn_xjone','layuiadmin-form-STU_ONE',null,function renderDoneFun(d){
          	
          });
      break;
      case 'syn_stuinfo':
    	  	layer.confirm('确定同步更新所选学生的学生信息吗？此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
  		  	  var checkStatus = table.checkStatus(obj.config.id) 
  		    	,checkData = checkStatus.data;//得到选中的数据
  		      if(checkData.length === 0){
  		      	return layer.msg('请选择数据');
  		      }
  		      var checkUids="";  
  		      layui.each(checkData, function(index, item){ 
  		  	  		checkUids+=item.STUDENT_NO+",";
  		  	  }); 
    	  		  var data1 = {stuNo:checkUids};
  	          easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/studentXjManage/flushStuInfo',data1,function successFun(res){
  	   	  		if(res.success){
  	   	  			$("#btn_stuInfoUid_search").click(); //刷新
  	   	    	}
  	   	  	  });
         	});
        break; 
      case 'batsyn_stuinfo':
  	  	layer.confirm('确定同步批量更新近3个学年的学生学籍信息吗？此操作不能撤销！', function(index) {
	          easyutils.reqDelete('easyajax/studentXjManage/executeXj',null,function successFun(res){
	   	  		if(res.success){
	   	  			$("#btn_stuNo_search").click(); //刷新
	   	    	}
	   	  	  });
       	});
      break;
    };
  });
  //监听行工具事件
  table.on('tool(easy-table-DORM_STUDENT_INFO)', function(obj){
    var data = obj.data;
    if(obj.event === 'edit'){
      	var data1 = {stuInfoUid:data.STU_INFO_UID};
      	easyutils.popupWindow("编辑",'50%','95%','dormstu/student/input','layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_INFO','easyajax/studentInfoManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
	        	
            });    
    } else if(obj.event === 'detail'){
    	var data1 = {stuInfoUid:data.STU_INFO_UID,isView:"1"};
    	easyutils.popupViewWindow("学生信息查看",'70%','95%','dormstu/student/view','layuiadmin-form-DORM_STUDENT_INFO','easyajax/studentInfoManage/getMap',data1,function renderDoneFun(d){
  			
        });
    }
  });

});

</script>

						         <p><strong>宿舍地址：</strong> <mdall id="stuSyn-DORM_ADDRESS"></mdall></p>
						       </div>
						    </div>
				       </div>
				    </div>
            	</div>

  </div>

<script>
layui.use(['admin', 'form', 'easyutils'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,admin = layui.admin
  ,form = layui.form
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils;

    easyutils.render(null,'layuiadmin-form-STU_ONE'); //初始化radio checkbox select 组件
    
  	$("#btn_search_stuSyn").click(function(){
  		var stuData = $("#SEARCH_STU_DORM_KEY").val();
  		if(stuData!=null && stuData!=''){
  			var data1 = {SEARCH_STU_DATA:stuData};
  	  	  	easyutils.reqGet('easyajax/stuDormManage/getStuDormMap',data1,function successFun(res){
  	  	  		if(res.success){
  	  	  			var successData=res.data;
  	  	  			easyutils.val("layuiadmin-form-STU_ONE",successData);
  	  	  			var dhtml = successData.GARDEN_NAME+successData.BUILDING_NAME+'栋'+successData.ROOM_NAME+'房'
  	  	  			dhtml+= '('+successData.ROOMTYPE_NAME+successData.ROOMTYPE_MONEY+'元)'
  	  	  		    $("#stuSyn-DORM_ADDRESS").html(dhtml);
  	  	  			easyutils.layMes('success',"操作成功！");
  	  		    }else{
  	  		    	easyutils.layMes('error',res.reasonremark);
  	    		    return false;
  	  		    }
  	  		}); 
  		}else{
  			 easyutils.layMes('error','请输入学号/考生号/身份证号数据！');
   		    return false;
  		}
    });
  	
  	$(document).keydown(function (e) {
		if (e.keyCode === 13) {
		  	$("#btn_search_stuSyn").trigger("click");
		}
	});
  	
});

</script>

<script>
layui.use(['form','easyutils'], function(){
  var $ = layui.$
  ,form = layui.form
  ,easyutils=layui.easyutils;
 
  easyutils.renderDateYear('layuiadmin-form-STU_SYN');
  easyutils.render(null,'layuiadmin-form-STU_SYN');
  
  //监听提交
  form.on('submit(LAY-STU_SYN-submit)', function(data){
    	var field = data.field; //获取提交的字段
    	layer.confirm("确定对该年级的学生数据进行同步？同步操作时会先删除之前的数据再进行同步", {icon: 3, title:'提示'},
            function(index){
	    		easyutils.reqSave('easyajax/synWelManage/synStu',field,function successFun(res){
	    			if(res.success){
	    				$("#btn_stuInfoUid_search").click();//刷新
	     			}
	    		});
         	layer.close(index);
        });
  });
  
  $("#btn_STU_SYN_close").click(function(){
 	 $("#admin-openw-close").click();//关闭弹窗
  });
  
  
});

</script>

  	  	  			var successData=res.data;
  	  	  			easyutils.val("layuiadmin-form-STU_ONE",successData);
  	  	  			easyutils.layMes('success',"操作成功！");
  	  		    }else{
  	  		    	easyutils.layMes('error',res.reasonremark);
  	    		    return false;
  	  		    }
  	  		}); 
  		}else{
  			 easyutils.layMes('error','请输入学号！');
   		    return false;
  		}
    });
  	
  	$(document).keydown(function (e) {
		if (e.keyCode === 13) {
		  	$("#btn_search_stuSyn").trigger("click");
		}
	});
  	
});

</script>

package com.easy.entity.dorm;

import java.util.Date;

import javax.persistence.Column;
import javax.persistence.Entity;
import javax.persistence.Id;

/**
* 宿舍床位表
*/
@Entity(name="DORM_BED")
public class DormBed implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	
	private Long bedUid;//
	private String bedName;//床位名称
	private Long roomUid;//房间ID
	private String bedStatus;//状态（0注销/1空位/2已住）
	private String bedRemark;//备注
	private String stuInfoUid;//入住学生ID
	private Date startDate;//入住时间
	private String bedstuRemark;//入住备注
	private Date updateTime;//修改时间
	private String updateUid;//修改人
	
	
	public DormBed() {
	}
	
	public DormBed(Long bedUid) {
		this.bedUid=bedUid;
	}
	
	public DormBed(Long bedUid,
	String bedName,
	Long roomUid,
	String bedStatus,
	String bedRemark,
	String stuInfoUid,
	Date startDate,
	String bedstuRemark,
	Date updateTime,
	String updateUid) {
		this.bedUid=bedUid;
		this.bedName=bedName;
		this.roomUid=roomUid;
		this.bedStatus=bedStatus;
		this.bedRemark=bedRemark;
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
		this.startDate=startDate;
		this.bedstuRemark=bedstuRemark;
		this.updateTime=updateTime;
		this.updateUid=updateUid;
	}
	
	@Id
	@Column(name = "BED_UID", unique = true, nullable = false, length = 22)
	public Long getBedUid(){
		return this.bedUid;
	}
	public void setBedUid(Long bedUid){
		this.bedUid=bedUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "BED_NAME")
	public String getBedName(){
		return this.bedName;
	}
	public void setBedName(String bedName){
		this.bedName=bedName;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_UID")
	public Long getRoomUid(){
		return this.roomUid;
	}
	public void setRoomUid(Long roomUid){
		this.roomUid=roomUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "BED_STATUS")
	public String getBedStatus(){
		return this.bedStatus;
	}
	public void setBedStatus(String bedStatus){
		this.bedStatus=bedStatus;
	}
	@Column(name = "BED_REMARK")
	public String getBedRemark(){
		return this.bedRemark;
	}
	public void setBedRemark(String bedRemark){
		this.bedRemark=bedRemark;
	}
	@Column(name = "STU_INFO_UID")
	public String getStuInfoUid(){
		return this.stuInfoUid;
	}
	public void setStuInfoUid(String stuInfoUid){
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "START_DATE")
	public Date getStartDate(){
		return this.startDate;
	}
	public void setStartDate(Date startDate){
		this.startDate=startDate;
	}
	
	@Column(name = "BEDSTU_REMARK")
	public String getBedstuRemark(){
		return this.bedstuRemark;
	}
	public void setBedstuRemark(String bedstuRemark){
		this.bedstuRemark=bedstuRemark;
	}
	@Column(name = "UPDATE_TIME")
	public Date getUpdateTime(){
		return this.updateTime;
	}
	public void setUpdateTime(Date updateTime){
		this.updateTime=updateTime;
	}
	@Column(name = "UPDATE_UID")
	public String getUpdateUid(){
		return this.updateUid;
	}
	public void setUpdateUid(String updateUid){
		this.updateUid=updateUid;
	}
	
}

package com.easy.entity.dorm;

import javax.persistence.Column;
import javax.persistence.Entity;
import javax.persistence.Id;

/**
* 宿舍楼宇表
*/
@Entity(name="DORM_BUILDING")
public class DormBuilding implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	
	private Long buildingUid;//
	private String buildingName;//名称
	private Long gardenUid;//园区ID
	private String buildingStatus;//状态
	private Integer floorCount;//楼层数据
	private String buildingAddress;//地址
	private String buildingRemark;//备注
	
	
	public DormBuilding() {
	}
	
	public DormBuilding(Long buildingUid) {
		this.buildingUid=buildingUid;
	}
	
	public DormBuilding(Long buildingUid,
	String buildingName,
	Long gardenUid,
	String buildingStatus,
	Integer floorCount,
	String buildingAddress,
	String buildingRemark) {
		this.buildingUid=buildingUid;
		this.buildingName=buildingName;
		this.gardenUid=gardenUid;
		this.buildingStatus=buildingStatus;
		this.floorCount=floorCount;
		this.buildingAddress=buildingAddress;
		this.buildingRemark=buildingRemark;
	}
	
	@Id
	@Column(name = "BUILDING_UID", unique = true, nullable = false, length = 22)
	public Long getBuildingUid(){
		return this.buildingUid;
	}
	public void setBuildingUid(Long buildingUid){
		this.buildingUid=buildingUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "BUILDING_NAME")
	public String getBuildingName(){
		return this.buildingName;
	}
	public void setBuildingName(String buildingName){
		this.buildingName=buildingName;
	}
	@Column(name = "GARDEN_UID")
	public Long getGardenUid(){
		return this.gardenUid;
	}
	public void setGardenUid(Long gardenUid){
		this.gardenUid=gardenUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "BUILDING_STATUS")
	public String getBuildingStatus(){
		return this.buildingStatus;
	}
	public void setBuildingStatus(String buildingStatus){
		this.buildingStatus=buildingStatus;
	}
	@Column(name = "FLOOR_COUNT")
	public Integer getFloorCount(){
		return this.floorCount;
	}
	public void setFloorCount(Integer floorCount){
		this.floorCount=floorCount;
	}
	@Column(name = "BUILDING_ADDRESS")
	public String getBuildingAddress(){
		return this.buildingAddress;
	}
	public void setBuildingAddress(String buildingAddress){
		this.buildingAddress=buildingAddress;
	}
	@Column(name = "BUILDING_REMARK")
	public String getBuildingRemark(){
		return this.buildingRemark;
	}
	public void setBuildingRemark(String buildingRemark){
		this.buildingRemark=buildingRemark;
	}
	
}

@Entity(name="DORM_CWFY")
public class DormCwfy implements java.io.Serializable {

	private String schoolYear;//学年
	private Long roomFee;//应缴住宿费
	private Long roomtypeMoney;//住宿标准价格
	private String cwfyStatus;//状态1已提交
	private Date createTime;//
	private String createUid;//
	private String cwfyNo;//传至财务系统流水号

	}
	
	public DormCwfy(Long cwfyUid) {

		this.cwfyType=cwfyType;
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;

		this.roomFee=roomFee;
		this.roomtypeMoney=roomtypeMoney;
		this.cwfyStatus=cwfyStatus;
		this.createTime=createTime;
		this.createUid=createUid;
		this.cwfyNo=cwfyNo;
	}

		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;

	public String getStudentNo(){

	}
	public void setStudentNo(String studentNo){
		this.studentNo=studentNo;
	}
	@Column(name = "SCHOOL_YEAR")

		return this.schoolYear;
	}

		this.schoolYear=schoolYear;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_FEE")

/**

@Entity(name="DORM_ROOM")
public class DormRoom implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;

	private String roomName;//名称
	private Integer bedCount;//床位数
	private Long floorUid;//楼层ID
	private String roomSex;//性别
	private String roomStatus;//状态(0:不启用1：已启用2：未启用)
	private String roomRemark;//备注
	private Long roomtypeUid;//房间标准类型
	
	
	public DormRoom() {
	}
	
	public DormRoom(Long roomUid) {
		this.roomUid=roomUid;
	}
	
	public DormRoom(Long roomUid,
	String roomName,
	Integer bedCount,
	Long floorUid,
	String roomSex,
	String roomStatus,
	String roomRemark,
	Long roomtypeUid) {
		this.roomUid=roomUid;
		this.roomName=roomName;
		this.bedCount=bedCount;
		this.floorUid=floorUid;
		this.roomSex=roomSex;
		this.roomStatus=roomStatus;
		this.roomRemark=roomRemark;
		this.roomtypeUid=roomtypeUid;
	}
	
	@Id
	@Column(name = "ROOM_UID", unique = true, nullable = false, length = 22)
	public Long getRoomUid(){
		return this.roomUid;
	}
	public void setRoomUid(Long roomUid){
		this.roomUid=roomUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_NAME")
	public String getRoomName(){
		return this.roomName;
	}
	public void setRoomName(String roomName){
		this.roomName=roomName;
	}
	@Column(name = "BED_COUNT")
	public Integer getBedCount(){
		return this.bedCount;
	}
	public void setBedCount(Integer bedCount){
		this.bedCount=bedCount;
	}
	@Column(name = "FLOOR_UID")
	public Long getFloorUid(){
		return this.floorUid;
	}
	public void setFloorUid(Long floorUid){
		this.floorUid=floorUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_SEX")
	public String getRoomSex(){
		return this.roomSex;
	}
	public void setRoomSex(String roomSex){
		this.roomSex=roomSex;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_STATUS")
	public String getRoomStatus(){
		return this.roomStatus;
	}
	public void setRoomStatus(String roomStatus){
		this.roomStatus=roomStatus;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_REMARK")
	public String getRoomRemark(){
		return this.roomRemark;
	}
	public void setRoomRemark(String roomRemark){
		this.roomRemark=roomRemark;

package com.easy.entity.dorm;

import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.util.Date;

import javax.persistence.Column;
import javax.persistence.Entity;
import javax.persistence.Id;

/**
* 宿舍房间水电记录
*/
@Entity(name="DORM_ROOM_MAINS")
public class DormRoomMains implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	
	private String mainsUid;//房间水电记录ID
	private String yearNum;//学年
	private String termNum;//学期
	private Long roomUid;//房间ID
	private Integer monthNumJm;//本条水电费减免月数（一学期减免5个月/一学年10个月）
	private Double waterNumHot;//热水表记录(底数)
	private Double waterNumCool;//冷水表记录(底数)
	private Double waterUse;//用水量
	private BigDecimal waterPrice;//水单价
	private BigDecimal waterFee;//应缴水费
	private Double electricBefore;//上次电表记录(前一次电表止码)
	private Double electricNum;//电表记录(底数)
	private Double electricUse;//用电量
	private BigDecimal electricPrice;//电单价
	private BigDecimal electricFee;//应缴电费
	private Date startDate;//开始日期
	private Date endDate;//截止日期
	private BigDecimal totalFee;//合计费（水费+电费）
	private Double oldElectricNum;//换电表时的旧表抄表记录
	private String mainsStatus;//状态1已提交0草稿
	private String createUid;//创建人ID
	private Date createTime;//创建时间
	private String updateUid;//修改人ID
	private Date updateTime;//修改时间
	private String mainsType;//水电收费类型(1国家标准2安宁校区标准3莲华校区标准
	
	
	public DormRoomMains() {
	}
	
	public DormRoomMains(String mainsUid) {
		this.mainsUid=mainsUid;
	}
	
	public DormRoomMains(String mainsUid,
	String yearNum,
	String termNum,
	Long roomUid,
	Integer monthNumJm,
	Double waterNumHot,
	Double waterNumCool,
	Double waterUse,
	BigDecimal waterPrice,
	BigDecimal waterFee,
	Double electricBefore,
	Double electricNum,
	Double electricUse,
	BigDecimal electricPrice,
	BigDecimal electricFee,
	Date startDate,
	Date endDate,
	BigDecimal totalFee,
	Double oldElectricNum,
	String mainsStatus,
	String createUid,
	Date createTime,
	String updateUid,
	Date updateTime,
	String mainsType) {
		this.mainsUid=mainsUid;
		this.yearNum=yearNum;
		this.termNum=termNum;
		this.roomUid=roomUid;
		this.monthNumJm=monthNumJm;
		this.waterNumHot=waterNumHot;
		this.waterNumCool=waterNumCool;
		this.waterUse=waterUse;
		this.waterPrice=waterPrice;
		this.waterFee=waterFee;
		this.electricBefore=electricBefore;
		this.electricNum=electricNum;
		this.electricUse=electricUse;
		this.electricPrice=electricPrice;
		this.electricFee=electricFee;
		this.startDate=startDate;
		this.endDate=endDate;
		this.totalFee=totalFee;
		this.oldElectricNum=oldElectricNum;
		this.mainsStatus=mainsStatus;
		this.createUid=createUid;
		this.createTime=createTime;
		this.updateUid=updateUid;
		this.updateTime=updateTime;
		this.mainsType=mainsType;
	}
	
	@Id
	@Column(name = "MAINS_UID", unique = true, nullable = false, length = 32)
	public String getMainsUid(){
		return this.mainsUid;
	}
	public void setMainsUid(String mainsUid){
		this.mainsUid=mainsUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "YEAR_NUM")
	public String getYearNum(){
		return this.yearNum;
	}
	public void setYearNum(String yearNum){
		this.yearNum=yearNum;
	}
	@Column(name = "TERM_NUM")
	public String getTermNum(){
		return this.termNum;
	}
	public void setTermNum(String termNum){
		this.termNum=termNum;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_UID")
	public Long getRoomUid(){
		return this.roomUid;
	}
	public void setRoomUid(Long roomUid){
		this.roomUid=roomUid;
	}
	
	@Column(name = "MONTH_NUM_JM")
	public Integer getMonthNumJm() {
		return monthNumJm;
	}

	public void setMonthNumJm(Integer monthNumJm) {
		this.monthNumJm = monthNumJm;
	}
	
	@Column(name = "WATER_NUM_HOT")
	public Double getWaterNumHot(){
		return this.waterNumHot;
	}
	public void setWaterNumHot(Double waterNumHot){
		this.waterNumHot=waterNumHot;
	}
	@Column(name = "WATER_NUM_COOL")
	public Double getWaterNumCool(){
		return this.waterNumCool;
	}
	public void setWaterNumCool(Double waterNumCool){
		this.waterNumCool=waterNumCool;
	}

		return this.waterPrice;
	}
	public void setWaterPrice(BigDecimal waterPrice){
		this.waterPrice=waterPrice;
	}

		return this.waterFee;
	}
	public void setWaterFee(BigDecimal waterFee){
		this.waterFee=waterFee;
	}

		this.electricBefore = electricBefore;

	}

	}

	}
	@Column(name = "UPDATE_TIME")
	public Date getUpdateTime(){
		return this.updateTime;
	}
	public void setUpdateTime(Date updateTime){
		this.updateTime=updateTime;
	}

	@Column(name = "MAINS_TYPE")
	public String getMainsType() {
		return mainsType;
	}
	public void setMainsType(String mainsType) {
		this.mainsType = mainsType;
	}
	
	
}

package com.easy.entity.dorm;

import java.math.BigDecimal;

/**
* 房间每位学生水电费明细
*/
@Entity(name="DORM_ROOM_MAINSSTU")
public class DormRoomMainsstu implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	
	private String mainsstuUid;//
	private String mainsUid;//宿舍房间水电记录id
	private String stumainsUid;//学生水电费UID(计算后反写过来)
	private Long roomUid;//房间ID
	private Long bedUid;//床位ID
	private String stuInfoUid;//学生ID
	private String studentNo;//学号
	private String yearNum;//学年
	private String termNum;//学期
	private Double waterUse;//用水量
	private BigDecimal waterPrice;//水单价
	private BigDecimal waterFee;//水费
	private Double electricUse;//用电量
	private BigDecimal electricPrice;//电单价
	private BigDecimal electricFee;//电费
	private Date startDate;//开始日期
	private Date endDate;//结束日期
	private String stumainsStatus;//状态0待提交 1已提交
	private String stumainsType;//交费类型(1正常住宿电费2退宿电费3宿舍调整电费
	private Date createTime;//费用生成时间
	private String createUid;//创建人
	private String updateUid;//
	private Date updateTime;//
	private String mainsType;
	private Integer monthStay;
	private BigDecimal monthElectric;
	private BigDecimal monthWater;
	
	public DormRoomMainsstu() {
	}
	
	public DormRoomMainsstu(String mainsstuUid) {
		this.mainsstuUid=mainsstuUid;
	}
	
	public DormRoomMainsstu(String mainsstuUid,
			String mainsUid,
			String stumainsUid,
	Long roomUid,
	Long bedUid,
	String stuInfoUid,
	String studentNo,
	String yearNum,
	String termNum,
	Double waterUse,
	BigDecimal waterPrice,
	BigDecimal waterFee,
	Double electricUse,
	BigDecimal electricPrice,
	BigDecimal electricFee,
	Date startDate,
	Date endDate,
	String stumainsStatus,
	String stumainsType,
	Date createTime,
	String createUid,
	String updateUid,
	Date updateTime,
	String mainsType,Integer monthStay,BigDecimal monthElectric,BigDecimal monthWater) {
		this.mainsstuUid=mainsstuUid;
		this.mainsUid=mainsUid;
		this.stumainsUid=stumainsUid;
		this.roomUid=roomUid;
		this.bedUid=bedUid;
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
		this.studentNo=studentNo;
		this.yearNum=yearNum;
		this.termNum=termNum;
		this.waterUse=waterUse;
		this.waterPrice=waterPrice;
		this.waterFee=waterFee;
		this.electricUse=electricUse;
		this.electricPrice=electricPrice;
		this.electricFee=electricFee;
		this.startDate=startDate;
		this.endDate=endDate;
		this.stumainsStatus=stumainsStatus;
		this.stumainsType=stumainsType;
		this.createTime=createTime;
		this.createUid=createUid;
		this.updateUid=updateUid;
		this.updateTime=updateTime;
		this.mainsType=mainsType;
		this.monthStay=monthStay;
		this.monthElectric=monthElectric;
		this.monthWater=monthWater;
	}

package com.easy.entity.dorm;

import java.math.BigDecimal;

import javax.persistence.Column;
import javax.persistence.Entity;
import javax.persistence.Id;

/**
* 学生水电费（计算周期水电费合计）
*/
@Entity(name="DORM_ROOM_STUMAINS")
public class DormRoomStumains implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	
	private String stumainsUid;//
	private String stuInfoUid;//学生ID
	private String studentNo;//学号
	private String yearNum;//学年
	private String termNum;//学期
	private Integer monthJmNum;//减免月数（一学期减免5个月/一学年10个月）
	private BigDecimal waterPrice;//水单价
	private BigDecimal waterFee;//水费
	private BigDecimal waterJmFee;//减免水费
	private BigDecimal electricPrice;//电单价
	private BigDecimal electricFee;//电费
	private BigDecimal electricJmFee;//减免电费
	private BigDecimal totalFee;//合计费用
	private Date startDate;//开始日期
	private Date endDate;//结束日期
	private String stumainsStatus;//状态（0待提交 1已提交
	private Date createTime;//费用生成时间
	private String createUid;//创建人
	private String serialNumber;//流水号(财务系统对接流水号)
	private String updateUid;//
	private Date updateTime;//
	private String mainsType;
	private Integer monthStay;
	
	
	public DormRoomStumains() {
	}
	
	public DormRoomStumains(String stumainsUid) {
		this.stumainsUid=stumainsUid;
	}
	
	public DormRoomStumains(String stumainsUid,
	String stuInfoUid,
	String studentNo,
	String yearNum,
	String termNum,
	Integer monthJmNum,
	BigDecimal waterPrice,
	BigDecimal waterFee,
	BigDecimal waterJmFee,
	BigDecimal electricPrice,
	BigDecimal electricFee,
	BigDecimal electricJmFee,
	BigDecimal totalFee,
	Date startDate,
	Date endDate,
	String stumainsStatus,
	Date createTime,
	String createUid,
	String serialNumber,
	String updateUid,
	Date updateTime,
	String mainsType,
	Integer monthStay) {
		this.stumainsUid=stumainsUid;
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
		this.studentNo=studentNo;
		this.yearNum=yearNum;
		this.termNum=termNum;
		this.monthJmNum=monthJmNum;
		this.waterPrice=waterPrice;
		this.waterFee=waterFee;
		this.waterJmFee=waterJmFee;
		this.electricPrice=electricPrice;
		this.electricFee=electricFee;
		this.electricJmFee=electricJmFee;
		this.totalFee=totalFee;
		this.startDate=startDate;
		this.endDate=endDate;
		this.stumainsStatus=stumainsStatus;
		this.createTime=createTime;
		this.createUid=createUid;
		this.serialNumber=serialNumber;
		this.updateUid=updateUid;
		this.updateTime=updateTime;
		this.mainsType=mainsType;
		this.monthStay=monthStay;
	}
	
	@Id
	@Column(name = "STUMAINS_UID", unique = true, nullable = false, length = 32)
	public String getStumainsUid(){
		return this.stumainsUid;
	}
	public void setStumainsUid(String stumainsUid){
		this.stumainsUid=stumainsUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "STU_INFO_UID")
	public String getStuInfoUid(){
		return this.stuInfoUid;
	}
	public void setStuInfoUid(String stuInfoUid){
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "STUDENT_NO")
	public String getStudentNo(){
		return this.studentNo;
	}
	public void setStudentNo(String studentNo){
		this.studentNo=studentNo;
	}
	@Column(name = "YEAR_NUM")
	public String getYearNum(){
		return this.yearNum;
	}
	public void setYearNum(String yearNum){
		this.yearNum=yearNum;
	}
	@Column(name = "TERM_NUM")
	public String getTermNum(){
		return this.termNum;
	}
	public void setTermNum(String termNum){
		this.termNum=termNum;
	}
	@Column(name = "MONTH_JM_NUM")

	}
	@Column(name = "WATER_PRICE")

		return this.waterPrice;

		this.waterPrice=waterPrice;

		this.waterFee=waterFee;

	}

	}
	@Column(name = "ELECTRIC_PRICE")

	}

		this.endDate=endDate;
	}

	}
	public void setStumainsStatus(String stumainsStatus){
		this.stumainsStatus=stumainsStatus;
	}
	@Column(name = "CREATE_TIME")
	public Date getCreateTime(){
		return this.createTime;
	}
	public void setCreateTime(Date createTime){
		this.createTime=createTime;
	}
	@Column(name = "CREATE_UID")
	public String getCreateUid(){
		return this.createUid;
	}
	public void setCreateUid(String createUid){
		this.createUid=createUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "SERIAL_NUMBER")
	public String getSerialNumber(){
		return this.serialNumber;
	}
	public void setSerialNumber(String serialNumber){
		this.serialNumber=serialNumber;
	}
	@Column(name = "UPDATE_UID")
	public String getUpdateUid(){
		return this.updateUid;
	}
	public void setUpdateUid(String updateUid){
		this.updateUid=updateUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "UPDATE_TIME")
	public Date getUpdateTime(){
		return this.updateTime;
	}
	public void setUpdateTime(Date updateTime){
		this.updateTime=updateTime;
	}
	@Column(name = "MAINS_TYPE")
	public String getMainsType() {
		return mainsType;
	}
	public void setMainsType(String mainsType) {
		this.mainsType = mainsType;
	}
	@Column(name = "MONTH_STAY")
	public Integer getMonthStay() {
		return monthStay;
	}
	public void setMonthStay(Integer monthStay) {
		this.monthStay = monthStay;
	}
