package com.easy.entity.dorm;

import java.util.Date;

import javax.persistence.Column;
import javax.persistence.Entity;
import javax.persistence.Id;

/**
* 学生床位费明细
*/
@Entity(name="DORM_STUDENT_BEDFEE")
public class DormStudentBedfee implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	
	private String bedfeeUid;//
	private String stuInfoUid;//学生ID
	private String studentNo;//学号
	private Long roomtypeMoney;//住宿标准价格
	private Integer monthsNum;//入住月数
	private Long monthMoney;//每月住宿费
	private String schoolYear;//学年
	private Long roomFee;//应缴住宿费
	private String bedfeeStatus;//状态1已提交2草稿
	private Date createTime;//创建时间
	private String createUid;//创建人
	private Date updateTime;//修改时间
	private String updateUid;//修改人
	private Long bedUid;//床位id
	private Date startDate;//开始时间
	private Date endDate;//结束时间
	
	
	public DormStudentBedfee() {
	}
	
	public DormStudentBedfee(String bedfeeUid) {
		this.bedfeeUid=bedfeeUid;
	}
	
	public DormStudentBedfee(String bedfeeUid,
	String stuInfoUid,
	String studentNo,
	Long roomtypeMoney,
	Integer monthsNum,
	Long monthMoney,
	String schoolYear,
	Long roomFee,
	String bedfeeStatus,
	Date createTime,
	String createUid,
	Date updateTime,
	String updateUid,
	Long bedUid,
	Date startDate,
	Date endDate) {
		this.bedfeeUid=bedfeeUid;
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
		this.studentNo=studentNo;
		this.roomtypeMoney=roomtypeMoney;
		this.monthsNum=monthsNum;
		this.monthMoney=monthMoney;
		this.schoolYear=schoolYear;
		this.roomFee=roomFee;
		this.bedfeeStatus=bedfeeStatus;
		this.createTime=createTime;
		this.createUid=createUid;
		this.updateTime=updateTime;
		this.updateUid=updateUid;
		this.bedUid=bedUid;
		this.startDate=startDate;
		this.endDate=endDate;
	}
	
	@Id
	@Column(name = "BEDFEE_UID", unique = true, nullable = false, length = 32)
	public String getBedfeeUid(){
		return this.bedfeeUid;
	}
	public void setBedfeeUid(String bedfeeUid){
		this.bedfeeUid=bedfeeUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "STU_INFO_UID")
	public String getStuInfoUid(){
		return this.stuInfoUid;
	}
	public void setStuInfoUid(String stuInfoUid){
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "STUDENT_NO")
	public String getStudentNo(){
		return this.studentNo;
	}
	public void setStudentNo(String studentNo){
		this.studentNo=studentNo;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOMTYPE_MONEY")
	public Long getRoomtypeMoney(){
		return this.roomtypeMoney;
	}
	public void setRoomtypeMoney(Long roomtypeMoney){
		this.roomtypeMoney=roomtypeMoney;
	}
	@Column(name = "MONTHS_NUM")
	public Integer getMonthsNum(){
		return this.monthsNum;
	}
	public void setMonthsNum(Integer monthsNum){
		this.monthsNum=monthsNum;
	}
	@Column(name = "MONTH_MONEY")
	public Long getMonthMoney(){
		return this.monthMoney;
	}
	public void setMonthMoney(Long monthMoney){
		this.monthMoney=monthMoney;
	}
	@Column(name = "SCHOOL_YEAR")
	public String getSchoolYear(){
		return this.schoolYear;
	}
	public void setSchoolYear(String schoolYear){
		this.schoolYear=schoolYear;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_FEE")
	public Long getRoomFee(){
		return this.roomFee;
	}
	public void setRoomFee(Long roomFee){
		this.roomFee=roomFee;
	}
	@Column(name = "BEDFEE_STATUS")
	public String getBedfeeStatus(){
		return this.bedfeeStatus;
	}
	public void setBedfeeStatus(String bedfeeStatus){
		this.bedfeeStatus=bedfeeStatus;
	}
	@Column(name = "CREATE_TIME")
	public Date getCreateTime(){
		return this.createTime;
	}
	public void setCreateTime(Date createTime){
		this.createTime=createTime;
	}
	@Column(name = "CREATE_UID")
	public String getCreateUid(){
		return this.createUid;
	}
	public void setCreateUid(String createUid){
		this.createUid=createUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "UPDATE_TIME")
	public Date getUpdateTime(){
		return this.updateTime;
	}
	public void setUpdateTime(Date updateTime){
		this.updateTime=updateTime;
	}
	@Column(name = "UPDATE_UID")
	public String getUpdateUid(){
		return this.updateUid;
	}
	public void setUpdateUid(String updateUid){
		this.updateUid=updateUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "BED_UID")
	public Long getBedUid(){
		return this.bedUid;
	}
	public void setBedUid(Long bedUid){
		this.bedUid=bedUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "START_DATE")
	public Date getStartDate(){
		return this.startDate;
	}
	public void setStartDate(Date startDate){
		this.startDate=startDate;
	}
	@Column(name = "END_DATE")
	public Date getEndDate(){
		return this.endDate;
	}
	public void setEndDate(Date endDate){
		this.endDate=endDate;
	}

/**
* 床位调整记录
*/
@Entity(name="DORM_STUDENT_BEDLOG")
public class DormStudentBedlog implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	
	private Long bedlogUid;//
	private Long bBedUid;//操作前床位ID
	private Integer bMonthsNum;//入住月数
	private Long bMonthMoney;//每月费用
	private Long aBedUid;//操作后床位ID
	private Integer aMonthsNum;//入住月数
	private Long aMonthMoney;//每月费用
	private String optUid;//操作人
	private Date optTime;//操作时间
	private String optRemark;//操作备注
	private String optContent;//操作内容
	private String stuInfoUid;
	private String optType;
	
	public DormStudentBedlog() {
	}
	
	public DormStudentBedlog(Long bedlogUid) {
		this.bedlogUid=bedlogUid;
	}
	
	public DormStudentBedlog(Long bedlogUid,
	Long bBedUid,
	Integer bMonthsNum,
	Long bMonthMoney,
	Long aBedUid,
	Integer aMonthsNum,
	Long aMonthMoney,
	String optUid,
	Date optTime,
	String optRemark,
	String optContent,String stuInfoUid,String optType) {
		this.bedlogUid=bedlogUid;
		this.bBedUid=bBedUid;
		this.bMonthsNum=bMonthsNum;
		this.bMonthMoney=bMonthMoney;
		this.aBedUid=aBedUid;
		this.aMonthsNum=aMonthsNum;
		this.aMonthMoney=aMonthMoney;
		this.optUid=optUid;
		this.optTime=optTime;
		this.optRemark=optRemark;
		this.optContent=optContent;
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
		this.optType=optType;
	}
	
	@Id
	@Column(name = "BEDLOG_UID", unique = true, nullable = false, length = 22)
	public Long getBedlogUid(){
		return this.bedlogUid;
	}
	public void setBedlogUid(Long bedlogUid){
		this.bedlogUid=bedlogUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "B_BED_UID")
	public Long getBBedUid(){
		return this.bBedUid;
	}
	public void setBBedUid(Long bBedUid){
		this.bBedUid=bBedUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "B_MONTHS_NUM")
	public Integer getBMonthsNum(){
		return this.bMonthsNum;
	}
	public void setBMonthsNum(Integer bMonthsNum){
		this.bMonthsNum=bMonthsNum;
	}
	@Column(name = "B_MONTH_MONEY")
	public Long getBMonthMoney(){
		return this.bMonthMoney;
	}
	public void setBMonthMoney(Long bMonthMoney){
		this.bMonthMoney=bMonthMoney;
	}
	@Column(name = "A_BED_UID")
	public Long getABedUid(){
		return this.aBedUid;
	}
	public void setABedUid(Long aBedUid){
		this.aBedUid=aBedUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "A_MONTHS_NUM")
	public Integer getAMonthsNum(){
		return this.aMonthsNum;
	}
	public void setAMonthsNum(Integer aMonthsNum){
		this.aMonthsNum=aMonthsNum;
	}
	@Column(name = "A_MONTH_MONEY")
	public Long getAMonthMoney(){
		return this.aMonthMoney;
	}
	public void setAMonthMoney(Long aMonthMoney){
		this.aMonthMoney=aMonthMoney;
	}
	@Column(name = "OPT_UID")
	public String getOptUid(){
		return this.optUid;
	}
	public void setOptUid(String optUid){
		this.optUid=optUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "OPT_TIME")
	public Date getOptTime(){
		return this.optTime;
	}
	public void setOptTime(Date optTime){
		this.optTime=optTime;
	}
	@Column(name = "OPT_REMARK")
	public String getOptRemark(){
		return this.optRemark;
	}
	public void setOptRemark(String optRemark){
		this.optRemark=optRemark;
	}
	@Column(name = "OPT_CONTENT")
	public String getOptContent(){
		return this.optContent;
	}
	public void setOptContent(String optContent){
		this.optContent=optContent;
	}
	@Column(name = "STU_INFO_UID")
	public String getStuInfoUid() {
		return stuInfoUid;
	}
	public void setStuInfoUid(String stuInfoUid) {
		this.stuInfoUid = stuInfoUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "OPT_TYPE")
	public String getOptType() {
		return optType;
	}
	public void setOptType(String optType) {
		this.optType = optType;
	}

	
}

package com.easy.entity.dorm;

import javax.persistence.Column;

/**
* 学生信息表
*/
@Entity(name="DORM_STUDENT_INFO")
public class DormStudentInfo implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	
	private String stuInfoUid;//记录ID（同USERID
	private String examineerUid;//考生号(同RECRUIT_STU_INFO表EXAMINEER_NO)
	private String registerUid;//报名号
	private String studentNo;//学生号
	private String studentName;//学生姓名
	private String cardNum;//身份证号
	private String sexCode;//性别代码（1男2女
	private String specialtyCode;//专业代码（校内专业）
	private String levelCode;//培养层次代码
	private String collegeCode;//院系代码
	private String nationCode;//民族代码
	private String classCode;//班级代码
	private String nationality;//国籍
	private String provinceCode;//生源地省
	private String cityCode;//生源地州市
	private String areaCode;//生源地区县
	private String politicalCode;//政治面貌代码
	private String xuezhiCode;//学制代码
	private String educationCode;//学历代码
	private String enrolDate;//入学日期
	private String leaveDate;//离校日期
	private String gradeCode;//年级
	private Integer istudentType;//状态1:新生2老生
	private String studentMemo;//备注
	private String registerStatus;//注册状态 1-未注册 2-已注册(退档状态：1退档/2未退档)
	private String schoolCode;//校区代码
	private String createTime;//添加（导入）时间
	
	
	public DormStudentInfo() {
	}
	
	public DormStudentInfo(String stuInfoUid) {
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
	}
	
	public DormStudentInfo(String stuInfoUid,
	String examineerUid,
	String registerUid,
	String studentNo,
	String studentName,
	String cardNum,
	String sexCode,
	String specialtyCode,
	String levelCode,
	String collegeCode,
	String nationCode,
	String classCode,
	String nationality,
	String provinceCode,
	String cityCode,
	String areaCode,
	String politicalCode,
	String xuezhiCode,
	String educationCode,
	String enrolDate,
	String leaveDate,
	String gradeCode,
	Integer istudentType,
	String studentMemo,
	String registerStatus,
	String schoolCode,
	String createTime) {
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
		this.examineerUid=examineerUid;
		this.registerUid=registerUid;
		this.studentNo=studentNo;
		this.studentName=studentName;
		this.cardNum=cardNum;
		this.sexCode=sexCode;
		this.specialtyCode=specialtyCode;
		this.levelCode=levelCode;
		this.collegeCode=collegeCode;
		this.nationCode=nationCode;
		this.classCode=classCode;
		this.nationality=nationality;
		this.provinceCode=provinceCode;
		this.cityCode=cityCode;
		this.areaCode=areaCode;
		this.politicalCode=politicalCode;
		this.xuezhiCode=xuezhiCode;
		this.educationCode=educationCode;
		this.enrolDate=enrolDate;
		this.leaveDate=leaveDate;
		this.gradeCode=gradeCode;
		this.istudentType=istudentType;
		this.studentMemo=studentMemo;
		this.registerStatus=registerStatus;
		this.schoolCode=schoolCode;
		this.createTime=createTime;
	}
	
	@Id
	@Column(name = "STU_INFO_UID", unique = true, nullable = false, length = 22)
	public String getStuInfoUid(){
		return this.stuInfoUid;
	}
	public void setStuInfoUid(String stuInfoUid){
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "EXAMINEER_UID")
	public String getExamineerUid(){
		return this.examineerUid;
	}
	public void setExamineerUid(String examineerUid){
		this.examineerUid=examineerUid;
	}

	}

	}

	@Column(name = "CARD_NUM")

package com.easy.entity.dorm;

import java.util.Date;

import javax.persistence.Column;
import javax.persistence.Entity;
import javax.persistence.Id;

/**
* 学生宿舍退宿表
*/
@Entity(name="DORM_STUDENT_RETURN")
public class DormStudentReturn implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	
	private Long returnUid;//
	private String stuInfoUid;//学生ID
	private Long bedUid;//床位id
	private String isReturn;//是否有退宿费用(0:批量退宿)
	private Long returnFree;//退宿费用
	private String returnStatus;//状态0:未定1:退房
	private String returnRemark;//备注
	private String createUid;//操作人员ID
	private Date createDate;//操作时间
	private String auditUid;//审批人员ID
	private Date auditTime;//审批时间
	private String returnType;//退宿类型(0不分摊水电/1分摊水电)
	private Date returnDate;//实际退宿日期
	
	public DormStudentReturn() {
	}
	
	public DormStudentReturn(Long returnUid) {
		this.returnUid=returnUid;
	}
	
	public DormStudentReturn(Long returnUid,
			String stuInfoUid,
	Long bedUid,
	String isReturn,
	Long returnFree,
	String returnStatus,
	String returnRemark,
	String createUid,
	Date createDate,
	String auditUid,
	Date auditTime,
	String returnType,Date returnDate) {
		this.returnUid=returnUid;
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
		this.bedUid=bedUid;
		this.isReturn=isReturn;
		this.returnFree=returnFree;
		this.returnStatus=returnStatus;
		this.returnRemark=returnRemark;
		this.createUid=createUid;
		this.createDate=createDate;
		this.auditUid=auditUid;
		this.auditTime=auditTime;
		this.returnType=returnType;
		this.returnDate=returnDate;
	}
	
	@Id
	@Column(name = "RETURN_UID", unique = true, nullable = false, length = 22)
	public Long getReturnUid(){
		return this.returnUid;
	}
	public void setReturnUid(Long returnUid){
		this.returnUid=returnUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "STU_INFO_UID")
	public String getStuInfoUid(){
		return this.stuInfoUid;
	}
	public void setStuInfoUid(String stuInfoUid){
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "BED_UID")
	public Long getBedUid(){
		return this.bedUid;
	}
	public void setBedUid(Long bedUid){
		this.bedUid=bedUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "IS_RETURN")
	public String getIsReturn(){
		return this.isReturn;
	}
	public void setIsReturn(String isReturn){
		this.isReturn=isReturn;
	}
	@Column(name = "RETURN_FREE")
	public Long getReturnFree(){
		return this.returnFree;
	}
	public void setReturnFree(Long returnFree){
		this.returnFree=returnFree;
	}
	@Column(name = "RETURN_STATUS")
	public String getReturnStatus(){
		return this.returnStatus;
	}
	public void setReturnStatus(String returnStatus){
		this.returnStatus=returnStatus;
	}
	@Column(name = "RETURN_REMARK")
	public String getReturnRemark(){
		return this.returnRemark;
	}
	public void setReturnRemark(String returnRemark){
		this.returnRemark=returnRemark;
	}
	@Column(name = "CREATE_UID")
	public String getCreateUid(){
		return this.createUid;
	}
	public void setCreateUid(String createUid){
		this.createUid=createUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "CREATE_DATE")
	public Date getCreateDate(){
		return this.createDate;
	}
	public void setCreateDate(Date createDate){
		this.createDate=createDate;
	}
	@Column(name = "AUDIT_UID")
	public String getAuditUid(){
		return this.auditUid;
	}
	public void setAuditUid(String auditUid){
		this.auditUid=auditUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "AUDIT_TIME")
	public Date getAuditTime(){
		return this.auditTime;
	}
	public void setAuditTime(Date auditTime){
		this.auditTime=auditTime;
	}
	@Column(name = "RETURN_TYPE")
	public String getReturnType() {
		return returnType;
	}
	public void setReturnType(String returnType) {
		this.returnType = returnType;
	}
	@Column(name = "RETURN_DATE")
	public Date getReturnDate() {
		return returnDate;
	}

	public void setReturnDate(Date returnDate) {
		this.returnDate = returnDate;
	}
	
	
}

package com.easy.entity.dorm;

import javax.persistence.Column;
import javax.persistence.Entity;
import javax.persistence.Id;
import java.util.Date;

/**
* 费用修改记录
*/
@Entity(name="DORM_UPDATE_HIS")
public class DormUpdateHis implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	
	private String dataUid;//ID
	private String dataType;//类型（zs 住宿费/sd 水电费）
	private String stuInfoUid;//学生信息ID
	private String studentNo;//学号
	private String schoolYear;//学年
	private String termNum;//学期
	private String roomFee;//费用金额
	private String dataRemark;//修改备注
	private Date updateTime;//
	private String updateUid;//
	
	
	public DormUpdateHis() {
	}
	
	public DormUpdateHis(String dataUid) {
		this.dataUid=dataUid;
	}
	
	public DormUpdateHis(String dataUid,
	String dataType,
	String stuInfoUid,
	String studentNo,
	String schoolYear,
	String termNum,
	String roomFee,
	String dataRemark,
	Date updateTime,
	String updateUid) {
		this.dataUid=dataUid;
		this.dataType=dataType;
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
		this.studentNo=studentNo;
		this.schoolYear=schoolYear;
		this.termNum=termNum;
		this.roomFee=roomFee;
		this.dataRemark=dataRemark;
		this.updateTime=updateTime;
		this.updateUid=updateUid;
	}
	
	@Id
	@Column(name = "DATA_UID", unique = true, nullable = false, length = 32)
	public String getDataUid(){
		return this.dataUid;
	}
	public void setDataUid(String dataUid){
		this.dataUid=dataUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "DATA_TYPE")
	public String getDataType(){
		return this.dataType;
	}
	public void setDataType(String dataType){
		this.dataType=dataType;
	}
	@Column(name = "STU_INFO_UID")
	public String getStuInfoUid(){
		return this.stuInfoUid;
	}
	public void setStuInfoUid(String stuInfoUid){
		this.stuInfoUid=stuInfoUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "STUDENT_NO")
	public String getStudentNo(){
		return this.studentNo;
	}
	public void setStudentNo(String studentNo){
		this.studentNo=studentNo;
	}
	@Column(name = "SCHOOL_YEAR")
	public String getSchoolYear(){
		return this.schoolYear;
	}
	public void setSchoolYear(String schoolYear){
		this.schoolYear=schoolYear;
	}
	@Column(name = "TERM_NUM")
	public String getTermNum(){
		return this.termNum;
	}
	public void setTermNum(String termNum){
		this.termNum=termNum;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_FEE")
	public String getRoomFee(){
		return this.roomFee;
	}
	public void setRoomFee(String roomFee){
		this.roomFee=roomFee;
	}
	@Column(name = "DATA_REMARK")
	public String getDataRemark(){
		return this.dataRemark;
	}
	public void setDataRemark(String dataRemark){
		this.dataRemark=dataRemark;
	}
	@Column(name = "UPDATE_TIME")
	public Date getUpdateTime(){
		return this.updateTime;
	}
	public void setUpdateTime(Date updateTime){
		this.updateTime=updateTime;
	}
	@Column(name = "UPDATE_UID")
	public String getUpdateUid(){
		return this.updateUid;
	}
	public void setUpdateUid(String updateUid){
		this.updateUid=updateUid;
	}
	
}

package com.easy.entity.dorm;

import java.util.Date;

import javax.persistence.Column;
import javax.persistence.Entity;
import javax.persistence.Id;

/**
* 迎新宿舍资源
*/
@Entity(name="DORM_WEL_CONTROL")
public class DormWelControl implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	
	private Long controlUid;//
	private Long bedUid;//床位ID
	private Long roomUid;//房间ID
	private String roomSex;//房间性别
	private Long roomtypeUid;//房间标准ID
	private String classCode;//班级代码
	private String createUid;//
	private Date createTime;//
	
	
	public DormWelControl() {
	}
	
	public DormWelControl(Long controlUid) {
		this.controlUid=controlUid;
	}
	
	public DormWelControl(Long controlUid,
	Long bedUid,
	Long roomUid,
	String roomSex,
	Long roomtypeUid,
	String classCode,
	String createUid,
	Date createTime) {
		this.controlUid=controlUid;
		this.bedUid=bedUid;
		this.roomUid=roomUid;
		this.roomSex=roomSex;
		this.roomtypeUid=roomtypeUid;
		this.classCode=classCode;
		this.createUid=createUid;
		this.createTime=createTime;
	}
	
	@Id
	@Column(name = "CONTROL_UID", unique = true, nullable = false, length = 22)
	public Long getControlUid(){
		return this.controlUid;
	}
	public void setControlUid(Long controlUid){
		this.controlUid=controlUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "BED_UID")
	public Long getBedUid(){
		return this.bedUid;
	}
	public void setBedUid(Long bedUid){
		this.bedUid=bedUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_UID")
	public Long getRoomUid(){
		return this.roomUid;
	}
	public void setRoomUid(Long roomUid){
		this.roomUid=roomUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_SEX")
	public String getRoomSex(){
		return this.roomSex;
	}
	public void setRoomSex(String roomSex){
		this.roomSex=roomSex;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOMTYPE_UID")
	public Long getRoomtypeUid(){
		return this.roomtypeUid;
	}
	public void setRoomtypeUid(Long roomtypeUid){
		this.roomtypeUid=roomtypeUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "CLASS_CODE")
	public String getClassCode(){
		return this.classCode;
	}
	public void setClassCode(String classCode){
		this.classCode=classCode;
	}
	@Column(name = "CREATE_UID")
	public String getCreateUid(){
		return this.createUid;
	}
	public void setCreateUid(String createUid){
		this.createUid=createUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "CREATE_TIME")
	public Date getCreateTime(){
		return this.createTime;
	}
	public void setCreateTime(Date createTime){
		this.createTime=createTime;
	}
	
}

package com.easy.entity.dorm;

import javax.persistence.Column;
import javax.persistence.Entity;
import javax.persistence.Id;

/**
* 
*/
@Entity(name="VIEW_DORM_ROOM")
public class ViewDormRoom implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	
	private Long gardenUid;//
	private String gardenName;//
	private String mainsType;
	private Long buildingUid;//
	private String buildingName;//
	private Long floorUid;//
	private String floorName;//
	private Long roomUid;//
	private String roomName;//
	private String roomSex;//
	private String roomStatus;//
	private Long roomtypeUid;//
	private String roomtypeName;//
	private Long roomtypeMoney;//
	private Integer stayMonths;//
	private Integer roomtypePresons;//
	private Long monthMoney;//
	
	
	public ViewDormRoom() {
		
	}

	
	@Id
	@Column(name = "ROOM_UID", unique = true, nullable = false, length = 22)
	public Long getRoomUid() {
		return roomUid;
	}
	public void setRoomUid(Long roomUid) {
		this.roomUid = roomUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_NAME")
	public String getRoomName() {
		return roomName;
	}
	public void setRoomName(String roomName) {
		this.roomName = roomName;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_SEX")
	public String getRoomSex() {
		return roomSex;
	}
	public void setRoomSex(String roomSex) {
		this.roomSex = roomSex;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOM_STATUS")
	public String getRoomStatus() {
		return roomStatus;
	}
	public void setRoomStatus(String roomStatus) {
		this.roomStatus = roomStatus;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOMTYPE_UID")
	public Long getRoomtypeUid() {
		return roomtypeUid;
	}
	public void setRoomtypeUid(Long roomtypeUid) {
		this.roomtypeUid = roomtypeUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOMTYPE_NAME")
	public String getRoomtypeName() {
		return roomtypeName;
	}
	public void setRoomtypeName(String roomtypeName) {
		this.roomtypeName = roomtypeName;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOMTYPE_MONEY")
	public Long getRoomtypeMoney() {
		return roomtypeMoney;
	}
	public void setRoomtypeMoney(Long roomtypeMoney) {
		this.roomtypeMoney = roomtypeMoney;
	}
	@Column(name = "STAY_MONTHS")
	public Integer getStayMonths() {
		return stayMonths;
	}
	public void setStayMonths(Integer stayMonths) {
		this.stayMonths = stayMonths;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOMTYPE_PRESONS")
	public Integer getRoomtypePresons() {
		return roomtypePresons;
	}
	public void setRoomtypePresons(Integer roomtypePresons) {
		this.roomtypePresons = roomtypePresons;
	}
	@Column(name = "MONTH_MONEY")
	public Long getMonthMoney() {
		return monthMoney;
	}
	public void setMonthMoney(Long monthMoney) {
		this.monthMoney = monthMoney;
	}
	@Column(name = "GARDEN_UID")
	public Long getGardenUid() {
		return gardenUid;
	}
	public void setGardenUid(Long gardenUid) {
		this.gardenUid = gardenUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "GARDEN_NAME")
	public String getGardenName() {
		return gardenName;
	}
	public void setGardenName(String gardenName) {
		this.gardenName = gardenName;
	}
	@Column(name = "BUILDING_UID")
	public Long getBuildingUid(){
		return buildingUid;
	}
	public void setBuildingUid(Long buildingUid) {
		this.buildingUid = buildingUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "BUILDING_NAME")
	public String getBuildingName() {
		return buildingName;
	}
	public void setBuildingName(String buildingName) {
		this.buildingName = buildingName;
	}
	@Column(name = "FLOOR_UID")
	public Long getFloorUid() {
		return floorUid;
	}
	public void setFloorUid(Long floorUid) {
		this.floorUid = floorUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "FLOOR_NAME")
	public String getFloorName() {
		return floorName;
	}
	public void setFloorName(String floorName) {
		this.floorName = floorName;
	}
	@Column(name = "MAINS_TYPE")
	public String getMainsType() {
		return mainsType;
	}
	public void setMainsType(String mainsType) {
		this.mainsType = mainsType;
	}
	
	
}	

package com.easy.entity.dorm;

import javax.persistence.Column;
import javax.persistence.Entity;
import javax.persistence.Id;

/**
* 
*/
@Entity(name="VIEW_DORM_SYS")
public class ViewDormSys implements java.io.Serializable {

	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;
	
	private Long gardenUid;//
	private String gardenName;//
	private Long buildingUid;//
	private String buildingName;//
	private Long floorUid;//
	private String floorName;//
	private Long roomUid;//
	private String roomName;//
	private String roomSex;//
	private String roomStatus;//
	private Long bedUid;//
	private String bedName;//
	private String bedStatus;//
	private Long roomtypeUid;//
	private String roomtypeName;//
	private Long roomtypeMoney;//
	private Integer stayMonths;//
	private Integer roomtypePresons;//
	private Long monthMoney;//
	
	
	public ViewDormSys() {
		
	}

	@Column(name = "GARDEN_UID")
	public Long getGardenUid() {
		return gardenUid;
	}
	public void setGardenUid(Long gardenUid) {
		this.gardenUid = gardenUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "GARDEN_NAME")
	public String getGardenName() {
		return gardenName;
	}
	public void setGardenName(String gardenName) {
		this.gardenName = gardenName;
	}
	@Column(name = "BUILDING_UID")
	public Long getBuildingUid(){
		return buildingUid;
	}
	public void setBuildingUid(Long buildingUid) {
		this.buildingUid = buildingUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "BUILDING_NAME")
	public String getBuildingName() {
		return buildingName;
	}
	public void setBuildingName(String buildingName) {
		this.buildingName = buildingName;
	}

		return floorUid;
	}

		this.floorUid = floorUid;
	}

		return floorName;
	}

		this.floorName = floorName;
	}

		return roomUid;
	}

		this.roomUid = roomUid;
	}

		return roomSex;

		this.roomSex = roomSex;
	}

		return roomStatus;
	}
	public void setRoomStatus(String roomStatus) {
		this.roomStatus = roomStatus;
	}

	@Id
	@Column(name = "BED_UID", unique = true, nullable = false, length = 22)
	public Long getBedUid() {
		return bedUid;
	}

		this.bedUid = bedUid;
	}

		return bedName;
	}

		this.bedName = bedName;
	}

		return bedStatus;
	}
	public void setBedStatus(String bedStatus) {
		this.bedStatus = bedStatus;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOMTYPE_UID")

		return roomtypeUid;
	}
	public void setRoomtypeUid(Long roomtypeUid) {
		this.roomtypeUid = roomtypeUid;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOMTYPE_NAME")
	public String getRoomtypeName() {
		return roomtypeName;
	}
	public void setRoomtypeName(String roomtypeName) {
		this.roomtypeName = roomtypeName;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOMTYPE_MONEY")
	public Long getRoomtypeMoney() {
		return roomtypeMoney;
	}
	public void setRoomtypeMoney(Long roomtypeMoney) {
		this.roomtypeMoney = roomtypeMoney;
	}
	@Column(name = "STAY_MONTHS")
	public Integer getStayMonths() {
		return stayMonths;
	}
	public void setStayMonths(Integer stayMonths) {
		this.stayMonths = stayMonths;
	}
	@Column(name = "ROOMTYPE_PRESONS")

		this.roomtypePresons = roomtypePresons;
	}

		return monthMoney;

		this.monthMoney = monthMoney;
	}
